  - [<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1046">Retarder la table du nom d’importation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1046">Delay Import Name Table</span></span>](#delay-import-name-table)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1047">Table d’adresses d’importation à liaison différée et horodatage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1047">Delay Bound Import Address Table and Time Stamp</span></span>](#delay-bound-import-address-table-and-time-stamp)
  - [<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1048">Différer la table d’adresses d’importation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1048">Delay Unload Import Address Table</span></span>](#delay-unload-import-address-table)

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1049">Les structures de données qui ont été décrites jusqu’à présent, jusqu’à et y compris l’en-tête facultatif, sont toutes situées à un décalage fixe par rapport au début du fichier (ou à partir de l’en-tête PE si le fichier est une image qui contient un stub MS-DOS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1049">The data structures that were described so far, up to and including the optional header, are all located at a fixed offset from the beginning of the file (or from the PE header if the file is an image that contains an MS-DOS stub).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1050">Le reste d’un fichier image ou objet COFF contient des blocs de données qui ne sont pas nécessairement à un décalage de fichier spécifique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1050">The remainder of a COFF object or image file contains blocks of data that are not necessarily at any specific file offset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1051">Au lieu de cela, les emplacements sont définis par des pointeurs dans l’en-tête facultatif ou un en-tête de section.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1051">Instead, the locations are defined by pointers in the optional header or a section header.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1052">Une exception concerne les images dont la valeur alignement de section est inférieure à la taille de page de l’architecture (4 K pour Intel x86 et pour MIPS, et 8 K pour Itanium).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1052">An exception is for images with a SectionAlignment value of less than the page size of the architecture (4 K for Intel x86 and for MIPS, and 8 K for Itanium).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1053">Pour obtenir une description de alignement de section, consultez l' [en-tête facultatif (image uniquement)](#optional-header-image-only).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1053">For a description of SectionAlignment, see [Optional Header (Image Only)](#optional-header-image-only).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1054">Dans ce cas, il existe des contraintes sur le décalage de fichier des données de la section, comme décrit dans la section 5,1, « données de la section ».</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1054">In this case, there are constraints on the file offset of the section data, as described in section 5.1, "Section Data."</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1055">Une autre exception est que le certificat d’attribut et les informations de débogage doivent être placés à la fin d’un fichier image, avec la table de certificats d’attribut qui précède immédiatement la section de débogage, car le chargeur ne les mappe pas en mémoire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1055">Another exception is that attribute certificate and debug information must be placed at the very end of an image file, with the attribute certificate table immediately preceding the debug section, because the loader does not map these into memory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1056">Toutefois, la règle relative au certificat d’attribut et aux informations de débogage ne s’applique pas aux fichiers objets.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1056">The rule about attribute certificate and debug information does not apply to object files, however.</span></span>

### <a name="section-data"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-1057">Données de la section</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1057">Section Data</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1058">Les données initialisées pour une section se composent de blocs d’octets simples.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1058">Initialized data for a section consists of simple blocks of bytes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1059">Toutefois, pour les sections qui contiennent des zéros, il n’est pas nécessaire d’inclure les données de la section.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1059">However, for sections that contain all zeros, the section data need not be included.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1060">Les données de chaque section se trouvent au niveau du décalage de fichier fourni par le champ PointerToRawData dans l’en-tête de la section.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1060">The data for each section is located at the file offset that was given by the PointerToRawData field in the section header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1061">La taille de ces données dans le fichier est indiquée par le champ SizeOfRawData.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1061">The size of this data in the file is indicated by the SizeOfRawData field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1062">Si SizeOfRawData est inférieur à VirtualSize, le reste est complété avec des zéros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1062">If SizeOfRawData is less than VirtualSize, the remainder is padded with zeros.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1063">Dans un fichier image, les données de la section doivent être alignées sur une limite telle que spécifiée par le champ assigne FileAlignment dans l’en-tête facultatif.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1063">In an image file, the section data must be aligned on a boundary as specified by the FileAlignment field in the optional header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1064">Les données de section doivent apparaître dans l’ordre des valeurs RVA pour les sections correspondantes (comme les en-têtes de section individuels dans la table de section).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1064">Section data must appear in order of the RVA values for the corresponding sections (as do the individual section headers in the section table).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1065">Il existe des restrictions supplémentaires sur les fichiers image si la valeur alignement de section dans l’en-tête facultatif est inférieure à la taille de page de l’architecture.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1065">There are additional restrictions on image files if the SectionAlignment value in the optional header is less than the page size of the architecture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1066">Pour ces fichiers, l’emplacement des données de section dans le fichier doit correspondre à son emplacement en mémoire lorsque l’image est chargée, afin que le décalage physique pour les données de section soit identique à l’adresse RVA.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1066">For such files, the location of section data in the file must match its location in memory when the image is loaded, so that the physical offset for section data is the same as the RVA.</span></span>

### <a name="coff-relocations-object-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-1067">Réadressages COFF (objet uniquement)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1067">COFF Relocations (Object Only)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1068">Les fichiers objets contiennent des réadressages COFF qui spécifient comment les données de la section doivent être modifiées lorsqu’elles sont placées dans le fichier image, puis chargées en mémoire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1068">Object files contain COFF relocations, which specify how the section data should be modified when placed in the image file and subsequently loaded into memory.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1069">Les fichiers image ne contiennent pas de réadressages COFF, car des adresses ont déjà été affectées à tous les symboles référencés dans un espace d’adressage plat.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1069">Image files do not contain COFF relocations, because all referenced symbols have already been assigned addresses in a flat address space.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1070">Une image contient des informations de réadressage sous la forme de réadressages de base dans la section. reloc (sauf si l’image a le \_ fichier image \_ des réadressages \_ attribut supprimé).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1070">An image contains relocation information in the form of base relocations in the .reloc section (unless the image has the IMAGE\_FILE\_RELOCS\_STRIPPED attribute).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1071">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [la section. reloc (image uniquement)](#the-reloc-section-image-only).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1071">For more information, see [The .reloc Section (Image Only)](#the-reloc-section-image-only).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1072">Pour chaque section d’un fichier objet, un tableau d’enregistrements de longueur fixe contient les réadressages COFF de la section.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1072">For each section in an object file, an array of fixed-length records holds the section's COFF relocations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1073">La position et la longueur du tableau sont spécifiées dans l’en-tête de la section.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1073">The position and length of the array are specified in the section header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1074">Chaque élément du tableau a le format suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1074">Each element of the array has the following format.</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1075">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1075">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1076">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1076">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1077">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1077">Field</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1078">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1078">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
|---------------|---------------|------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1079">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1079">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1080">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1080">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1081">VirtualAddress</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1081">VirtualAddress</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1082">Adresse de l’élément auquel la réadressage est appliquée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1082">The address of the item to which relocation is applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1083">Il s’agit du décalage à partir du début de la section, plus la valeur du champ RVA/offset de la section.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1083">This is the offset from the beginning of the section, plus the value of the section's RVA/Offset field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1084">Consultez la [section table (en-têtes de section)](#section-table-section-headers).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1084">See [Section Table (Section Headers)](#section-table-section-headers).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1085">Par exemple, si le premier octet de la section a l’adresse 0x10, le troisième octet a une adresse de 0x12.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1085">For example, if the first byte of the section has an address of 0x10, the third byte has an address of 0x12.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1086">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1086">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1087">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1087">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1088">SymbolTableIndex</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1088">SymbolTableIndex</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1089">Index de base zéro dans la table de symboles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1089">A zero-based index into the symbol table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1090">Ce symbole indique l’adresse à utiliser pour le déplacement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1090">This symbol gives the address that is to be used for the relocation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1091">Si le symbole spécifié a une classe de stockage de section, l’adresse du symbole est l’adresse avec la première section du même nom.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1091">If the specified symbol has section storage class, then the symbol's address is the address with the first section of the same name.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                 |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1092">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1092">8</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1093">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1093">2</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1094">Type</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1094">Type</span></span> <br/>             | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1095">Valeur qui indique le type de réadressage qui doit être effectué.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1095">A value that indicates the kind of relocation that should be performed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1096">Les types de réadressage valides dépendent du type d’ordinateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1096">Valid relocation types depend on machine type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1097">Consultez [indicateurs de type](#type-indicators).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1097">See [Type Indicators](#type-indicators).</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                     |



 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1098">Si le symbole référencé par le champ SymbolTableIndex a la section Storage Class IMAGE \_ sym \_ Class \_ , l’adresse du symbole est le début de la section.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1098">If the symbol referred to by the SymbolTableIndex field has the storage class IMAGE\_SYM\_CLASS\_SECTION, the symbol's address is the beginning of the section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1099">La section se trouve généralement dans le même fichier, sauf si le fichier objet fait partie d’une archive (bibliothèque).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1099">The section is usually in the same file, except when the object file is part of an archive (library).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1100">Dans ce cas, la section se trouve dans tout autre fichier objet de l’archive qui a le même nom de membre d’archive que le fichier objet actuel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1100">In that case, the section can be found in any other object file in the archive that has the same archive-member name as the current object file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1101">(La relation avec le nom du membre d’archive est utilisée dans la liaison des tables d’importation, autrement dit, la section. idata.)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1101">(The relationship with the archive-member name is used in the linking of import tables, that is, the .idata section.)</span></span>

#### <a name="type-indicators"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-1102">Indicateurs de type</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1102">Type Indicators</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1103">Le champ type de l’enregistrement de réadressage indique le type de réadressage à effectuer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1103">The Type field of the relocation record indicates what kind of relocation should be performed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1104">Différents types de réadressage sont définis pour chaque type d’ordinateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1104">Different relocation types are defined for each type of machine.</span></span>

##### <a name="intel-itanium-processor-family-ipf"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-1480">Intel Itanium Processor Family (IPF)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1480">Intel Itanium Processor Family (IPF)</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1585">\_ \_ Jeton ia64 d’image rel \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1585">IMAGE\_REL\_IA64\_TOKEN</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1586">0x001b</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1586">0x001b</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1587">Jeton CLR.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1587">A CLR token.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1588">IMAGE \_ rel \_ ia64 \_ GPREL32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1588">IMAGE\_REL\_IA64\_GPREL32</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1589">0x001c</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1589">0x001c</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1590">Correction relative à GP 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1590">A 32-bit GP-relative fixup.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1591">IMAGE \_ rel \_ ia64 \_ ADDEND</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1591">IMAGE\_REL\_IA64\_ADDEND</span></span> <br/>     | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1592">0x001F</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1592">0x001F</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1593">Le déplacement est valide uniquement lorsqu’il suit immédiatement l’un des réadressages suivants : IMM14, IMM22, IMM64, GPREL22, LTOFF22, LTOFF64, SECREL22, SECREL64I ou SECREL32.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1593">The relocation is valid only when it immediately follows one of the following relocations: IMM14, IMM22, IMM64, GPREL22, LTOFF22, LTOFF64, SECREL22, SECREL64I, or SECREL32.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1594">Sa valeur contient le addend à appliquer aux instructions dans un bundle, et non aux données.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1594">Its value contains the addend to apply to instructions within a bundle, not for data.</span></span> <br/>                                                                  |

| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1686">IMAGE \_ rel \_ m32r \_ REFHI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1686">IMAGE\_REL\_M32R\_REFHI</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1687">0x0009</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1687">0x0009</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1688">16 MSBs du VA cible, ajusté pour l’extension de signe LSB.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1688">The 16 MSBs of the target VA, adjusted for LSB sign extension.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1689">Elle est utilisée pour la première instruction dans une séquence à deux instructions qui charge une adresse 32 bits complète.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1689">This is used for the first instruction in a two-instruction sequence that loads a full 32-bit address.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1690">Ce réadressage doit être immédiatement suivi d’un réadressage de paire dont SymbolTableIndex contient un déplacement 16 bits signé qui est ajouté aux 16 bits supérieurs qui sont tirés de l’emplacement en cours de déplacement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1690">This relocation must be immediately followed by a PAIR relocation whose SymbolTableIndex contains a signed 16-bit displacement that is added to the upper 16 bits that are taken from the location that is being relocated.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1691">IMAGE \_ rel \_ m32r \_ REFLO</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1691">IMAGE\_REL\_M32R\_REFLO</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1692">0x000A</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1692">0x000A</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1693">16 LSBs du VA cible.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1693">The 16 LSBs of the target VA.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1694">\_ \_ Paire m32r d' \_ image</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1694">IMAGE\_REL\_M32R\_PAIR</span></span> <br/>     | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1695">0x000B</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1695">0x000B</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1696">Le réadressage doit suivre le réadressage REFHI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1696">The relocation must follow the REFHI relocation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1697">Son SymbolTableIndex contient un déplacement et non un index dans la table de symboles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1697">Its SymbolTableIndex contains a displacement and not an index into the symbol table.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1698">IMAGE \_ rel \_ m32r \_ section</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1698">IMAGE\_REL\_M32R\_SECTION</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1699">0x000C</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1699">0x000C</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1700">Index de la section 16 bits de la section qui contient la cible.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1700">The 16-bit section index of the section that contains the target.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1701">Utilisé pour prendre en charge les informations de débogage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1701">This is used to support debugging information.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                  |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1702">IMAGE \_ rel \_ m32r \_ SECREL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1702">IMAGE\_REL\_M32R\_SECREL</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1703">0x000D</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1703">0x000D</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1704">Offset 32 bits de la cible à partir du début de sa section.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1704">The 32-bit offset of the target from the beginning of its section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1705">Cela permet de prendre en charge les informations de débogage et le stockage local des threads statiques.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1705">This is used to support debugging information and static thread local storage.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1706">\_ \_ Jeton m32r d’image rel \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1706">IMAGE\_REL\_M32R\_TOKEN</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1707">0x000E</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1707">0x000E</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1708">Jeton CLR.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1708">The CLR token.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |



 

### <a name="coff-line-numbers-deprecated"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-1709">Numéros de ligne COFF (déconseillé)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1709">COFF Line Numbers (Deprecated)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1710">Les numéros de ligne COFF ne sont plus produits et, à l’avenir, ne sont pas consommés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1710">COFF line numbers are no longer produced and, in the future, will not be consumed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1711">Les numéros de ligne COFF indiquent la relation entre le code et les numéros de ligne dans les fichiers sources.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1711">COFF line numbers indicate the relationship between code and line numbers in source files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1712">Le format Microsoft pour les numéros de ligne COFF est semblable au format COFF standard, mais il a été étendu pour permettre à une section unique d’être liée à des numéros de ligne dans plusieurs fichiers sources.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1712">The Microsoft format for COFF line numbers is similar to standard COFF, but it has been extended to allow a single section to relate to line numbers in multiple source files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1713">Les numéros de ligne COFF se composent d’un tableau d’enregistrements de longueur fixe.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1713">COFF line numbers consist of an array of fixed-length records.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1714">L’emplacement (décalage de fichier) et la taille du tableau sont spécifiés dans l’en-tête de la section.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1714">The location (file offset) and size of the array are specified in the section header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1715">Chaque enregistrement de numéro de ligne est au format suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1715">Each line-number record is of the following format.</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1716">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1716">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1717">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1717">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1718">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1718">Field</span></span>                  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1719">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1719">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                 |
|---------------|---------------|------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1720">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1720">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1721">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1721">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1722">Type ( \* )</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1722">Type (\*)</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1723">Il s’agit d’une Union de deux champs : SymbolTableIndex et VirtualAddress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1723">This is a union of two fields: SymbolTableIndex and VirtualAddress.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1724">L’utilisation de SymbolTableIndex ou d’un RVA dépend de la valeur de LineNumber.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1724">Whether SymbolTableIndex or RVA is used depends on the value of Linenumber.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1725">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1725">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1726">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1726">2</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1727">LineNumber</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1727">Linenumber</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1728">Si la valeur est différente de zéro, ce champ spécifie un numéro de ligne de base 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1728">When nonzero, this field specifies a one-based line number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1729">Lorsque la valeur est égale à zéro, le champ de type est interprété comme un index de table de symboles pour une fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1729">When zero, the Type field is interpreted as a symbol table index for a function.</span></span> <br/>    |



 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1730">Le champ de type est une Union de champs de 2 4 octets : SymbolTableIndex et VirtualAddress.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1730">The Type field is a union of two 4-byte fields: SymbolTableIndex and VirtualAddress.</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1731">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1731">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1732">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1732">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1733">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1733">Field</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1734">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1734">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                             |
|---------------|---------------|------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1735">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1735">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1736">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1736">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1737">SymbolTableIndex</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1737">SymbolTableIndex</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1738">Utilisé lorsque LineNumber est égal à zéro : index de l’entrée de table de symboles pour une fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1738">Used when Linenumber is zero: index to symbol table entry for a function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1739">Ce format est utilisé pour indiquer la fonction à laquelle un groupe d’enregistrements de numéro de ligne fait référence.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1739">This format is used to indicate the function to which a group of line-number records refers.</span></span> <br/>      |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1740">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1740">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1741">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1741">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1742">VirtualAddress</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1742">VirtualAddress</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1743">Utilisé lorsque LineNumber est différent de zéro : l’adresse RVA du code exécutable qui correspond à la ligne source indiquée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1743">Used when Linenumber is non-zero: the RVA of the executable code that corresponds to the source line indicated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1744">Dans un fichier objet, contient le VA dans la section.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1744">In an object file, this contains the VA within the section.</span></span> <br/> |



 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1745">Un enregistrement de numéro de ligne peut affecter la valeur zéro au champ LineNumber et pointer vers une définition de fonction dans la table de symboles, ou il peut fonctionner comme une entrée de numéro de ligne standard en donnant un entier positif (numéro de ligne) et l’adresse correspondante dans le code de l’objet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1745">A line-number record can either set the Linenumber field to zero and point to a function definition in the symbol table or it can work as a standard line-number entry by giving a positive integer (line number) and the corresponding address in the object code.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1746">Un groupe d’entrées de numéro de ligne commence toujours par le premier format : l’index d’un symbole de fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1746">A group of line-number entries always begins with the first format: the index of a function symbol.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1747">S’il s’agit du premier enregistrement de numéro de ligne dans la section, il s’agit également du nom de symbole COMDAT pour la fonction si l’indicateur COMDAT de la section est défini.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1747">If this is the first line-number record in the section, then it is also the COMDAT symbol name for the function if the section's COMDAT flag is set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1748">Consultez les [sections COMDAT (objet uniquement)](#comdat-sections-object-only).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1748">See [COMDAT Sections (Object Only)](#comdat-sections-object-only).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1749">L’enregistrement auxiliaire de la fonction dans la table de symboles a un pointeur vers le champ LineNumber qui pointe vers ce même enregistrement de numéro de ligne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1749">The function's auxiliary record in the symbol table has a pointer to the Linenumber field that points to this same line-number record.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1750">Un enregistrement qui identifie une fonction est suivi d’un nombre quelconque d’entrées de numéro de ligne qui fournissent des informations de numéro de ligne réelles (c’est-à-dire des entrées avec LineNumber supérieur à zéro).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1750">A record that identifies a function is followed by any number of line-number entries that give actual line-number information (that is, entries with Linenumber greater than zero).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1751">Ces entrées sont de base un, par rapport au début de la fonction, et représentent chaque ligne source dans la fonction à l’exception de la première ligne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1751">These entries are one-based, relative to the beginning of the function, and represent every source line in the function except for the first line.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1752">Par exemple, le premier enregistrement de numéro de ligne de l’exemple suivant spécifie la fonction ReverseSign (SymbolTableIndex de ReverseSign et LineNumber ayant la valeur zéro).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1752">For example, the first line-number record for the following example would specify the ReverseSign function (SymbolTableIndex of ReverseSign and Linenumber set to zero).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1753">Ensuite, les enregistrements avec les valeurs LineNumber 1, 2 et 3 se suivent, correspondant aux lignes sources, comme indiqué ci-dessous :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1753">Then records with Linenumber values of 1, 2, and 3 would follow, corresponding to source lines as shown:</span></span>


```C++
// some code precedes ReverseSign function
int ReverseSign(int i)
1: {
2:  return -1 * i;
3: }
```



### <a name="coff-symbol-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-1754">Table de symboles COFF</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1754">COFF Symbol Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1755">La table de symboles de cette section est héritée du format COFF traditionnel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1755">The symbol table in this section is inherited from the traditional COFF format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1756">Il est différent de Microsoft Visual C++ informations de débogage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1756">It is distinct from Microsoft Visual C++ debug information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1757">Un fichier peut contenir à la fois une table de symboles COFF et Visual C++ informations de débogage, et les deux sont conservés séparément.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1757">A file can contain both a COFF symbol table and Visual C++ debug information, and the two are kept separate.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1758">Certains outils Microsoft utilisent la table de symboles à des fins limitées mais importantes, telles que la communication des informations COMDAT à l’éditeur de liens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1758">Some Microsoft tools use the symbol table for limited but important purposes, such as communicating COMDAT information to the linker.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1759">Les noms de section et les noms de fichiers, ainsi que les symboles de code et de données, sont répertoriés dans la table de symboles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1759">Section names and file names, as well as code and data symbols, are listed in the symbol table.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1760">L’emplacement de la table de symboles est indiqué dans l’en-tête COFF.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1760">The location of the symbol table is indicated in the COFF header.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1761">La table de symboles est un tableau d’enregistrements, dont la longueur est de 18 octets.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1761">The symbol table is an array of records, each 18 bytes long.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1762">Chaque enregistrement est un enregistrement de table de symboles standard ou auxiliaire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1762">Each record is either a standard or auxiliary symbol-table record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1763">Un enregistrement standard définit un symbole ou un nom et a le format suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1763">A standard record defines a symbol or name and has the following format.</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1764">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1764">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1765">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1765">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1766">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1766">Field</span></span>                          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1767">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1767">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
|----------------|---------------|--------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1768">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1768">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1769">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1769">8</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1770">Name ( \* )</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1770">Name (\*)</span></span> <br/>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1771">Nom du symbole, représenté par une Union de trois structures.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1771">The name of the symbol, represented by a union of three structures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1772">Un tableau de 8 octets est utilisé si le nom ne dépasse pas 8 octets.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1772">An array of 8 bytes is used if the name is not more than 8 bytes long.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1773">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [représentation du nom de symbole](https://www.bing.com/search?q=Symbol+Name+Representation).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1773">For more information, see [Symbol Name Representation](https://www.bing.com/search?q=Symbol+Name+Representation).</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1774">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1774">8</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1775">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1775">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1776">Valeur</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1776">Value</span></span> <br/>              | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1777">Valeur associée au symbole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1777">The value that is associated with the symbol.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1778">L’interprétation de ce champ dépend de SectionNumber et de StorageClass.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1778">The interpretation of this field depends on SectionNumber and StorageClass.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1779">Une signification type est l’adresse réadressable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1779">A typical meaning is the relocatable address.</span></span> <br/>                                                         |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1780">12</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1780">12</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1781">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1781">2</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1782">SectionNumber</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1782">SectionNumber</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1783">Entier signé qui identifie la section, à l’aide d’un index de base un dans la table de section.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1783">The signed integer that identifies the section, using a one-based index into the section table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1784">Certaines valeurs ont une signification particulière, telle que définie dans la section 5.4.2, « valeurs des numéros de section ».</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1784">Some values have special meaning, as defined in section 5.4.2, "Section Number Values."</span></span> <br/>                                         |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1785">14</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1785">14</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1786">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1786">2</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1787">Type</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1787">Type</span></span> <br/>               | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1788">Nombre qui représente le type.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1788">A number that represents type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1789">Les outils Microsoft définissent ce champ sur 0x20 (Function) ou 0x0 (pas une fonction).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1789">Microsoft tools set this field to 0x20 (function) or 0x0 (not a function).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1790">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [représentation de type](#type-representation).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1790">For more information, see [Type Representation](#type-representation).</span></span> <br/>                                                |

| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1796">17</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1796">17</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1797">1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1797">1</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1798">NumberOfAuxSymbols</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1798">NumberOfAuxSymbols</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1799">Nombre d’entrées de table de symboles auxiliaires qui suivent cet enregistrement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1799">The number of auxiliary symbol table entries that follow this record.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                           |



 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1800">Zéro, un ou plusieurs enregistrements de table de symboles auxiliaires suivent immédiatement chaque enregistrement de table de symboles standard.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1800">Zero or more auxiliary symbol-table records immediately follow each standard symbol-table record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1801">Toutefois, en général, il n’est pas plus d’un enregistrement de table de symboles auxiliaire qui suit un enregistrement de table de symboles standard (à l’exception des enregistrements. file avec des noms de fichiers longs).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1801">However, typically not more than one auxiliary symbol-table record follows a standard symbol-table record (except for .file records with long file names).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1802">Chaque enregistrement auxiliaire est de la même taille qu’un enregistrement de table de symboles standard (18 octets), mais au lieu de définir un nouveau symbole, l’enregistrement auxiliaire fournit des informations supplémentaires sur le dernier symbole défini.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1802">Each auxiliary record is the same size as a standard symbol-table record (18 bytes), but rather than define a new symbol, the auxiliary record gives additional information on the last symbol defined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1803">Le choix des formats à utiliser dépend du champ StorageClass.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1803">The choice of which of several formats to use depends on the StorageClass field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1804">Les formats actuellement définis pour les enregistrements de table de symboles auxiliaires sont indiqués dans la section 5,5, « enregistrements de symboles auxiliaires ».</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1804">Currently-defined formats for auxiliary symbol table records are shown in section 5.5, "Auxiliary Symbol Records."</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1805">Les outils qui lisent les tables de symboles COFF doivent ignorer les enregistrements de symboles auxiliaires dont l’interprétation est inconnue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1805">Tools that read COFF symbol tables must ignore auxiliary symbol records whose interpretation is unknown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1806">Cela permet d’étendre le format de table de symboles pour ajouter de nouveaux enregistrements auxiliaires, sans arrêter les outils existants.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1806">This allows the symbol table format to be extended to add new auxiliary records, without breaking existing tools.</span></span>

#### <a name="symbol-name-representation"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-1807">Représentation du nom de symbole</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1807">Symbol Name Representation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1808">Le champ ShortName dans une table de symboles se compose de 8 octets qui contiennent le nom lui-même, s’il n’est pas supérieur à 8 octets, ou si le champ ShortName donne un décalage dans la table de chaînes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1808">The ShortName field in a symbol table consists of 8 bytes that contain the name itself, if it is not more than 8 bytes long, or the ShortName field gives an offset into the string table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1809">Pour déterminer si le nom lui-même ou un décalage est donné, testez les 4 premiers octets pour obtenir une égalité égale à zéro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1809">To determine whether the name itself or an offset is given, test the first 4 bytes for equality to zero.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1810">Par Convention, les noms sont traités comme des chaînes encodées en UTF-8 se terminant par zéro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1810">By convention, the names are treated as zero-terminated UTF-8 encoded strings.</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1811">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1811">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1812">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1812">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1813">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1813">Field</span></span>                 | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1814">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1814">Description</span></span>                                                                                                          |
|---------------|---------------|-----------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1815">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1815">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1816">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1816">8</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1817">NomCourt</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1817">ShortName</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1818">Tableau de 8 octets.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1818">An array of 8 bytes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1819">Ce tableau est complété avec des valeurs NULL à droite si le nom comporte moins de 8 octets.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1819">This array is padded with nulls on the right if the name is less than 8 bytes long.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1820">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1820">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1821">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1821">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1822">Zéros</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1822">Zeroes</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1823">Champ défini sur tous les zéros si le nom comporte plus de 8 octets.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1823">A field that is set to all zeros if the name is longer than 8 bytes.</span></span> <br/>                                     |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1824">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1824">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1825">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1825">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1826">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1826">Offset</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1827">Offset dans la table de chaînes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1827">An offset into the string table.</span></span> <br/>                                                                         |



 

#### <a name="section-number-values"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-1828">Valeurs des numéros de section</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1828">Section Number Values</span></span>

#### <a name="type-representation"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-1847">Représentation de type</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1847">Type Representation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1848">Le champ de type d’une entrée de table de symboles contient 2 octets, où chaque octet représente des informations de type.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1848">The Type field of a symbol table entry contains 2 bytes, where each byte represents type information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1849">LSB représente le type de données simple (base) et l’MSB représente le type complexe, le cas échéant :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1849">The LSB represents the simple (base) data type, and the MSB represents the complex type, if any:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1850">MSB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1850">MSB</span></span>                                                       | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1851">LSB</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1851">LSB</span></span>                                                        |
|-----------------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1852">Type complexe : aucun, pointeur, fonction, tableau.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1852">Complex type: none, pointer, function, array.</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1853">Type de base : entier, virgule flottante, etc.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1853">Base type: integer, floating-point, and so on.</span></span> <br/> |



 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1854">Les valeurs suivantes sont définies pour le type de base, bien que les outils Microsoft n’utilisent généralement pas ce champ et attribuent à LSB la valeur 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1854">The following values are defined for base type, although Microsoft tools generally do not use this field and set the LSB to 0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1855">Au lieu de cela, les informations de débogage Visual C++ sont utilisées pour indiquer les types.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1855">Instead, Visual C++ debug information is used to indicate types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1856">Toutefois, les valeurs COFF possibles sont répertoriées ici à des fins d’exhaustivité.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1856">However, the possible COFF values are listed here for completeness.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1909">L’octet le plus significatif spécifie si le symbole est un pointeur vers, un retour de fonction ou un tableau du type de base qui est spécifié dans le LSB.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1909">The most significant byte specifies whether the symbol is a pointer to, function returning, or array of the base type that is specified in the LSB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1910">Les outils Microsoft utilisent ce champ uniquement pour indiquer si le symbole est une fonction, de sorte que les deux seules valeurs résultantes sont 0x0 et 0x20 pour le champ de type.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1910">Microsoft tools use this field only to indicate whether the symbol is a function, so that the only two resulting values are 0x0 and 0x20 for the Type field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1911">Toutefois, d’autres outils peuvent utiliser ce champ pour communiquer plus d’informations.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1911">However, other tools can use this field to communicate more information.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1912">Il est très important de spécifier correctement l’attribut de fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1912">It is very important to specify the function attribute correctly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1913">Ces informations sont nécessaires pour que les liens incrémentiels fonctionnent correctement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1913">This information is required for incremental linking to work correctly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1914">Pour certaines architectures, les informations peuvent être requises à d’autres fins.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1914">For some architectures, the information may be required for other purposes.</span></span>

#### <a name="storage-class"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-1930">Classe de stockage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1930">Storage Class</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1931">Le champ StorageClass de la table de symboles indique le type de définition représenté par un symbole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1931">The StorageClass field of the symbol table indicates what kind of definition a symbol represents.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1932">Le tableau suivant indique les valeurs possibles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1932">The following table shows possible values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1933">Notez que le champ StorageClass est un entier non signé sur 1 octet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1933">Note that the StorageClass field is an unsigned 1-byte integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1934">La valeur spéciale-1 doit donc être prise pour signifier son équivalent non signé, 0xFF.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1934">The special value -1 should therefore be taken to mean its unsigned equivalent, 0xFF.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-1935">Bien que le format COFF traditionnel utilise de nombreuses valeurs de classe de stockage, les outils Microsoft s’appuient sur Visual C++ format de débogage pour la plupart des informations symboliques et utilisent généralement uniquement quatre valeurs de classe de stockage : externe (2), statique (3), fonction (101) et fichier (103).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1935">Although the traditional COFF format uses many storage-class values, Microsoft tools rely on Visual C++ debug format for most symbolic information and generally use only four storage-class values: EXTERNAL (2), STATIC (3), FUNCTION (101), and FILE (103).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-1936">Sauf dans le deuxième en-tête de colonne ci-dessous, « valeur » doit être utilisé pour signifier le champ de valeur de l’enregistrement de symboles (dont l’interprétation dépend du nombre trouvé comme classe de stockage).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-1936">Except in the second column heading below, "Value" should be taken to mean the Value field of the symbol record (whose interpretation depends on the number found as the storage class).</span></span>

BB (début de bloc) ou. LF, le champ valeur indique le nombre de lignes sources dans la fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2018">For .lf records, the Value field gives the number of source lines in the function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2019">Pour les enregistrements. EF, le champ valeur indique la taille du code de la fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2019">For .ef records, the Value field gives the size of the function code.</span></span> <br/> |

### <a name="auxiliary-symbol-records"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2039">Enregistrements de symboles auxiliaires</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2039">Auxiliary Symbol Records</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2040">Les enregistrements de table de symboles auxiliaires suivent toujours, et s’appliquent à, un enregistrement de table de symboles standard.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2040">Auxiliary symbol table records always follow, and apply to, some standard symbol table record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2041">Un enregistrement auxiliaire peut avoir n’importe quel format que les outils peuvent reconnaître, mais 18 octets doivent leur être alloués afin que la table de symboles soit gérée comme un tableau de taille normale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2041">An auxiliary record can have any format that the tools can recognize, but 18 bytes must be allocated for them so that symbol table is maintained as an array of regular size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2042">Actuellement, les outils Microsoft reconnaissent les formats auxiliaires pour les types d’enregistrements suivants : les définitions de fonction, les symboles de début et de fin de fonction (. BF et. EF), les externes faibles, les noms de fichiers et les définitions de section.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2042">Currently, Microsoft tools recognize auxiliary formats for the following kinds of records: function definitions, function begin and end symbols (.bf and .ef), weak externals, file names, and section definitions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2043">La conception COFF traditionnelle comprend également des formats d’enregistrement auxiliaires pour les tableaux et les structures.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2043">The traditional COFF design also includes auxiliary-record formats for arrays and structures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2044">Les outils Microsoft n’utilisent pas ceux-ci, mais placent plutôt ces informations symboliques dans Visual C++ format de débogage dans les sections de débogage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2044">Microsoft tools do not use these, but instead place that symbolic information in Visual C++ debug format in the debug sections.</span></span>

#### <a name="auxiliary-format-1-function-definitions"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2045">Format auxiliaire 1 : définitions de fonction</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2045">Auxiliary Format 1: Function Definitions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2046">Un enregistrement de table de symboles marque le début d’une définition de fonction s’il a tous les éléments suivants : une classe de stockage externe (2), une valeur de type qui indique qu’il s’agit d’une fonction (0x20) et d’un numéro de section supérieur à zéro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2046">A symbol table record marks the beginning of a function definition if it has all of the following: a storage class of EXTERNAL (2), a Type value that indicates it is a function (0x20), and a section number that is greater than zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2047">Notez qu’un enregistrement de table de symboles ayant un numéro de section non défini (0) ne définit pas la fonction et n’a pas d’enregistrement auxiliaire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2047">Note that a symbol table record that has a section number of UNDEFINED (0) does not define the function and does not have an auxiliary record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2048">Les enregistrements de symboles de définition de fonction sont suivis d’un enregistrement auxiliaire dans le format décrit ci-dessous :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2048">Function-definition symbol records are followed by an auxiliary record in the format described below:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2049">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2049">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2050">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2050">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2051">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2051">Field</span></span>                             | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2052">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2052">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
|----------------|---------------|-----------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2053">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2053">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2054">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2054">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2055">TagIndex</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2055">TagIndex</span></span> <br/>              | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2056">Index de table de symboles de l’enregistrement de symbole. BF (Begin Function) correspondant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2056">The symbol-table index of the corresponding .bf (begin function) symbol record.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                   |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2057">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2057">4</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2058">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2058">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2059">TotalSize</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2059">TotalSize</span></span> <br/>             | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2060">Taille du code exécutable de la fonction elle-même.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2060">The size of the executable code for the function itself.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2061">Si la fonction est dans sa propre section, le SizeOfRawData dans l’en-tête de la section est supérieur ou égal à ce champ, selon les considérations d’alignement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2061">If the function is in its own section, the SizeOfRawData in the section header is greater or equal to this field, depending on alignment considerations.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2062">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2062">8</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2063">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2063">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2064">PointerToLinenumber</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2064">PointerToLinenumber</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2065">Décalage de fichier de la première entrée de numéro de ligne COFF pour la fonction, ou zéro si aucune n’existe.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2065">The file offset of the first COFF line-number entry for the function, or zero if none exists.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2066">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [numéros de ligne COFF (déconseillé)](#coff-line-numbers-deprecated).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2066">For more information, see [COFF Line Numbers (Deprecated)](#coff-line-numbers-deprecated).</span></span> <br/>                          |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2067">12</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2067">12</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2068">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2068">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2069">PointerToNextFunction</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2069">PointerToNextFunction</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2070">Index de table de symboles de l’enregistrement pour la fonction suivante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2070">The symbol-table index of the record for the next function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2071">Si la fonction est la dernière dans la table de symboles, ce champ a la valeur zéro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2071">If the function is the last in the symbol table, this field is set to zero.</span></span> <br/>                                                                           |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2072">16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2072">16</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2073">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2073">2</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2074">Inutilisé</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2074">Unused</span></span> <br/>                |                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |



 

#### <a name="auxiliary-format-2-bf-and-ef-symbols"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2075">Format auxiliaire 2 : symboles. BF et. EF</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2075">Auxiliary Format 2: .bf and .ef Symbols</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2076">Pour chaque définition de fonction dans la table de symboles, trois éléments décrivent le début, la fin et le nombre de lignes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2076">For each function definition in the symbol table, three items describe the beginning, ending, and number of lines.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2077">Chacun de ces symboles a une fonction de classe de stockage (101) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2077">Each of these symbols has storage class FUNCTION (101):</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2078">Un enregistrement de symbole nommé. BF (fonction Begin).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2078">A symbol record named .bf (begin function).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2079">Le champ de valeur n’est pas utilisé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2079">The Value field is unused.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2080">Enregistrement de symbole nommé. LF (lignes dans la fonction).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2080">A symbol record named .lf (lines in function).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2081">Le champ valeur indique le nombre de lignes dans la fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2081">The Value field gives the number of lines in the function.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2082">Un enregistrement de symbole nommé. EF (End of Function).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2082">A symbol record named .ef (end of function).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2083">Le champ de valeur a le même nombre que le champ Taille totale de l’enregistrement de symboles de définition de fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2083">The Value field has the same number as the Total Size field in the function-definition symbol record.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2084">Les enregistrements de symboles. BF et. EF (mais pas les enregistrements. LF) sont suivis d’un enregistrement auxiliaire au format suivant :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2084">The .bf and .ef symbol records (but not .lf records) are followed by an auxiliary record with the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2085">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2085">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2086">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2086">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2087">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2087">Field</span></span>                                         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2088">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2088">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                   |
|----------------|---------------|-----------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2089">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2089">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2090">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2090">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2091">Inutilisé</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2091">Unused</span></span> <br/>                            |                                                                                                                                                                               |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2092">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2092">4</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2093">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2093">2</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2094">LineNumber</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2094">Linenumber</span></span> <br/>                        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2095">Nombre réel de lignes ordinales (1, 2, 3, etc.) dans le fichier source, correspondant à l’enregistrement. BF ou. EF.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2095">The actual ordinal line number (1, 2, 3, and so on) within the source file, corresponding to the .bf or .ef record.</span></span> <br/>                                               |

BF uniquement)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2101">PointerToNextFunction ( .bf only)</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2102">Index de table de symboles de l’enregistrement de symbole BF suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2102">The symbol-table index of the next .bf symbol record.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2103">Si la fonction est la dernière dans la table de symboles, ce champ a la valeur zéro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2103">If the function is the last in the symbol table, this field is set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2104">Elle n’est pas utilisée pour les enregistrements.
