| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2618">\_type de débogage d’image \_ \_ FPO</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2618">IMAGE\_DEBUG\_TYPE\_FPO</span></span> <br/>             | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2619">3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2619">3</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2620">Informations d’omission du pointeur de frame (FPO).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2620">The frame pointer omission (FPO) information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2621">Ces informations indiquent au débogueur comment interpréter les frames de pile non standard, qui utilisent le registre EBP à une autre fin que comme pointeur de frame.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2621">This information tells the debugger how to interpret nonstandard stack frames, which use the EBP register for a purpose other than as a frame pointer.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2622">\_type de débogage d’image \_ \_ misc</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2622">IMAGE\_DEBUG\_TYPE\_MISC</span></span> <br/>            | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2623">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2623">4</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2624">Emplacement du fichier DBG.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2624">The location of DBG file.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2625">\_exception de type de débogage d’image \_ \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2625">IMAGE\_DEBUG\_TYPE\_EXCEPTION</span></span> <br/>       | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2626">5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2626">5</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2627">Copie de la section. pData.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2627">A copy of .pdata section.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2628">\_Correction du type de débogage de l’image \_ \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2628">IMAGE\_DEBUG\_TYPE\_FIXUP</span></span> <br/>           | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2629">6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2629">6</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2630">Réservé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2630">Reserved.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2631">\_ \_ type de débogage d’image \_ OMAP \_ vers \_ src</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2631">IMAGE\_DEBUG\_TYPE\_OMAP\_TO\_SRC</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2632">7</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2632">7</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2633">Mappage d’un RVA dans image à un RVA dans l’image source.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2633">The mapping from an RVA in image to an RVA in source image.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                          |

| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2640">\_Type de débogage d’image \_ \_ RESERVED10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2640">IMAGE\_DEBUG\_TYPE\_RESERVED10</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2641">10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2641">10</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2642">Réservé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2642">Reserved.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2643">\_type de débogage d’image \_ \_ CLSID</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2643">IMAGE\_DEBUG\_TYPE\_CLSID</span></span> <br/>           | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2644">11</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2644">11</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2645">Réservé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2645">Reserved.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2646">\_reproduction de type de débogage d’image \_ \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2646">IMAGE\_DEBUG\_TYPE\_REPRO</span></span> <br/>           | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2647">16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2647">16</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2648">Déterminisme ou reproductibilité PE.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2648">PE determinism or reproducibility.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                   |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2649">\_type de débogage d’image \_ \_ ex \_ DLLCHARACTERISTICS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2649">IMAGE\_DEBUG\_TYPE\_EX\_DLLCHARACTERISTICS</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2650">20</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2650">20</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2651">Caractéristiques des DLL étendues.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2651">Extended DLL characteristics bits.</span></span> |



 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2652">Si le champ type est défini sur IMAGE \_ Debug \_ type \_ FPO, les données brutes de débogage sont un tableau dans lequel chaque membre décrit le frame de pile d’une fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2652">If the Type field is set to IMAGE\_DEBUG\_TYPE\_FPO, the debug raw data is an array in which each member describes the stack frame of a function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2653">Toutes les fonctions du fichier image ne doivent pas avoir d’informations FPO définies, même si le type de débogage est FPO.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2653">Not every function in the image file must have FPO information defined for it, even though debug type is FPO.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2654">Les fonctions qui n’ont pas d’informations FPO sont supposées avoir des frames de pile normaux.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2654">Those functions that do not have FPO information are assumed to have normal stack frames.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2655">Le format des informations FPO est le suivant :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2655">The format for FPO information is as follows:</span></span>


```C++
#define FRAME_FPO   0               
#define FRAME_TRAP  1
#define FRAME_TSS   2
               
typedef struct _FPO_DATA {
    DWORD       ulOffStart;            // offset 1st byte of function code
    DWORD       cbProcSize;            // # bytes in function
    DWORD       cdwLocals;             // # bytes in locals/4
    WORD        cdwParams;             // # bytes in params/4
    WORD        cbProlog : 8;          // # bytes in prolog
    WORD        cbRegs   : 3;          // # regs saved
    WORD        fHasSEH  : 1;          // TRUE if SEH in func
    WORD        fUseBP   : 1;          // TRUE if EBP has been allocated
    WORD        reserved : 1;          // reserved for future use
    WORD        cbFrame  : 2;          // frame type
} FPO_DATA;
```



<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2656">La présence d’une entrée de type IMAGE de \_ débogage de type \_ \_ reproduction indique que le fichier PE est généré de manière à atteindre le déterminisme ou la reproductibilité.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2656">The presence of an entry of type IMAGE\_DEBUG\_TYPE\_REPRO indicates the PE file is built in a way to achieve determinism or reproducibility.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2657">Si l’entrée n’est pas modifiée, le fichier PE de sortie est garanti comme étant un bit-bit identique, quel que soit l’endroit où le PE est produit.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2657">If the input does not change, the output PE file is guaranteed to be bit-for-bit identical no matter when or where the PE is produced.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2658">Divers champs de datage de date et d’heure dans le fichier PE sont remplis avec une partie ou l’ensemble des bits d’une valeur de hachage calculée qui utilise le contenu de fichier PE comme entrée, et par conséquent, ne représentent plus la date et l’heure réelles auxquelles un fichier PE ou des données spécifiques associées dans le PE sont produits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2658">Various date/time stamp fields in the PE file are filled with part or all the bits from a calculated hash value that uses PE file content as input, and therefore no longer represent the actual date and time when a PE file or related specific data within the PE is produced.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2659">Les données brutes de cette entrée de débogage peuvent être vides ou peuvent contenir une valeur de hachage calculée précédée d’une valeur de quatre octets qui représente la longueur de la valeur de hachage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2659">The raw data of this debug entry may be empty, or may contain a calculated hash value preceded by a four-byte value that represents the hash value length.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2660">Si le champ type est défini sur IMAGE \_ Debug \_ type \_ ex \_ DLLCHARACTERISTICS, les données brutes de débogage contiennent des bits de caractéristiques de dll étendues, en plus de celles qui peuvent être définies dans l’en-tête facultatif de l’image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2660">If the Type field is set to IMAGE\_DEBUG\_TYPE\_EX\_DLLCHARACTERISTICS, the debug raw data contains extended DLL characteristics bits, in additional to those that could be set in image’s optional header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2661">Consultez les caractéristiques de la [dll](#dll-characteristics) dans la section [en-tête facultatif Windows-Specific champs (image uniquement)](#optional-header-windows-specific-fields-image-only).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2661">See [DLL Characteristics](#dll-characteristics) in section [Optional Header Windows-Specific Fields (Image Only)](#optional-header-windows-specific-fields-image-only).</span></span>

##### <a name="extended-dll-characteristics"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2662">Caractéristiques des DLL étendues</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2662">Extended DLL Characteristics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2663">Les valeurs suivantes sont définies pour les bits de caractéristiques de la DLL étendue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2663">The following values are defined for the extended DLL characteristics bits.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2664">Constante</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2664">Constant</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2665">Valeur</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2665">Value</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2666">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2666">Description</span></span> |
|-|-|-|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2667">IMAGE \_ DLLCHARACTERISTICS \_ ex \_ . \_ compatibilité</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2667">IMAGE\_DLLCHARACTERISTICS\_EX\_CET\_COMPAT</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2668">0x0001</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2668">0x0001</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2669">L’image est compatible avec l’heure d’été.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2669">Image is CET compatible.</span></span> |

#### <a name="debugf-object-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2670">. Debug $ F (objet uniquement)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2670">.debug$F (Object Only)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2671">Les données de cette section ont été remplacées dans Visual C++ version 7,0 et les versions ultérieures par un ensemble plus complet de données émises dans une sous-section **$ S Debug** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2671">The data in this section has been superseded in Visual C++ version 7.0 and later by a more extensive set of data that is emitted into a **.debug$S** subsection.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2672">Les fichiers objets peuvent contenir des sections. Debug $ F dont le contenu est un ou plusieurs \_ enregistrements de données FPO (informations d’omission du pointeur de frame).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2672">Object files can contain .debug$F sections whose contents are one or more FPO\_DATA records (frame pointer omission information).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2673">Consultez « IMAGE \_ Debug \_ type \_ FPO » dans [type de débogage](#debug-type).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2673">See "IMAGE\_DEBUG\_TYPE\_FPO" in [Debug Type](#debug-type).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2674">L’éditeur de liens reconnaît ces enregistrements **. Debug $ F** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2674">The linker recognizes these **.debug$F** records.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2675">Si des informations de débogage sont générées, l’éditeur de liens trie les \_ enregistrements de données FPO par RVA de procédure et génère une entrée de répertoire de débogage pour eux.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2675">If debug information is being generated, the linker sorts the FPO\_DATA records by procedure RVA and generates a debug directory entry for them.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2676">Le compilateur ne doit pas générer d’enregistrements FPO pour les procédures qui ont un format de cadre standard.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2676">The compiler should not generate FPO records for procedures that have a standard frame format.</span></span>

#### <a name="debugs-object-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2677">. déboguer $ S (objet uniquement)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2677">.debug$S (Object Only)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2678">Cette section contient Visual C++ informations de débogage (informations symboliques).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2678">This section contains Visual C++ debug information (symbolic information).</span></span>

#### <a name="debugp-object-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2679">. Debug $ P (objet uniquement)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2679">.debug$P (Object Only)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2680">Cette section contient Visual C++ informations de débogage (informations précompilées).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2680">This section contains Visual C++ debug information (precompiled information).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2681">Il s’agit de types partagés parmi tous les objets qui ont été compilés à l’aide de l’en-tête précompilé qui a été généré avec cet objet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2681">These are shared types among all of the objects that were compiled by using the precompiled header that was generated with this object.</span></span>

#### <a name="debugt-object-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2682">. Debug $ T (objet uniquement)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2682">.debug$T (Object Only)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2683">Cette section contient Visual C++ informations de débogage (informations de type).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2683">This section contains Visual C++ debug information (type information).</span></span>

#### <a name="linker-support-for-microsoft-debug-information"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2684">Prise en charge de l’éditeur de liens pour les informations de débogage Microsoft</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2684">Linker Support for Microsoft Debug Information</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2685">Pour prendre en charge les informations de débogage, l’éditeur de liens :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2685">To support debug information, the linker:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2686">Rassemble toutes les données de débogage pertinentes à partir des sections **. Debug $ F**, **Debug $ S**, **. Debug $ P** et **. Debug $ T** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2686">Gathers all relevant debug data from the **.debug$F**, **debug$S**, **.debug$P**, and **.debug$T** sections.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2687">Traite ces données avec les informations de débogage générées par l’éditeur de liens dans le fichier PDB et crée une entrée de répertoire de débogage pour y faire référence.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2687">Processes that data along with the linker-generated debugging information into the PDB file, and creates a debug directory entry to refer to it.</span></span>

### <a name="the-drectve-section-object-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2688">Section. drectve (objet uniquement)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2688">The .drectve Section (Object Only)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2689">Une section est une section de directive si elle possède l' \_ \_ Indicateur SCN LNK \_ info défini dans l’en-tête de la section et a le nom de la section **. drectve** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2689">A section is a directive section if it has the IMAGE\_SCN\_LNK\_INFO flag set in the section header and has the **.drectve** section name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2690">L’éditeur de liens supprime une section **. drectve** après avoir traité les informations, donc la section n’apparaît pas dans le fichier image qui est lié.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2690">The linker removes a **.drectve** section after processing the information, so the section does not appear in the image file that is being linked.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2691">Une section **. drectve** se compose d’une chaîne de texte qui peut être encodée au format ANSI ou UTF-8.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2691">A **.drectve** section consists of a string of text that can be encoded as ANSI or UTF-8.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2692">Si le marqueur d’ordre d’octet UTF-8 (BOM, un préfixe de trois octets qui se compose de 0xEF, 0xBB et 0xBF) n’est pas présent, la chaîne de directive est interprétée comme ANSI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2692">If the UTF-8 byte order marker (BOM, a three-byte prefix that consists of 0xEF, 0xBB, and 0xBF) is not present, the directive string is interpreted as ANSI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2693">La chaîne de directive est une série d’options de l’éditeur de liens séparées par des espaces.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2693">The directive string is a series of linker options that are separated by spaces.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2694">Chaque option contient un trait d’Union, le nom de l’option et tout attribut approprié.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2694">Each option contains a hyphen, the option name, and any appropriate attribute.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2695">Si une option contient des espaces, l’option doit être placée entre guillemets.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2695">If an option contains spaces, the option must be enclosed in quotes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2696">La section **. drectve** ne doit pas avoir de réadressages ou de numéros de ligne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2696">The **.drectve** section must not have relocations or line numbers.</span></span>

### <a name="the-edata-section-image-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2697">Section. edata (image uniquement)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2697">The .edata Section (Image Only)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2698">La section Export Data, nommée. edata, contient des informations sur les symboles auxquels d’autres images peuvent accéder via la liaison dynamique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2698">The export data section, named .edata, contains information about symbols that other images can access through dynamic linking.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2699">Les symboles exportés se trouvent généralement dans les dll, mais les dll peuvent également importer des symboles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2699">Exported symbols are generally found in DLLs, but DLLs can also import symbols.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2700">Une vue d’ensemble de la structure générale de la section exportation est décrite ci-dessous.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2700">An overview of the general structure of the export section is described below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2701">Les tables décrites sont généralement contiguës dans le fichier dans l’ordre indiqué (bien que cela ne soit pas obligatoire).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2701">The tables described are usually contiguous in the file in the order shown (though this is not required).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2702">Seule la table d’exportation et la table d’adresses d’exportation sont requises pour exporter les symboles en tant qu’ordinaux.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2702">Only the export directory table and export address table are required to export symbols as ordinals.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2703">(Un ordinal est une exportation accessible directement par son index de table d’adresses d’exportation.) La table de pointeur de nom, la table ordinale et la table de noms d’exportation existent pour prendre en charge l’utilisation des noms d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2703">(An ordinal is an export that is accessed directly by its export address table index.) The name pointer table, ordinal table, and export name table all exist to support use of export names.</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2704">Nom de la table</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2704">Table Name</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2705">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2705">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
|------------------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2706">Exporter une table de répertoire</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2706">Export directory table</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2707">Table avec une seule ligne (contrairement au répertoire de débogage).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2707">A table with just one row (unlike the debug directory).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2708">Ce tableau indique les emplacements et les tailles des autres tables d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2708">This table indicates the locations and sizes of the other export tables.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2709">Exporter une table d’adresses</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2709">Export address table</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2710">Tableau de RVA des symboles exportés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2710">An array of RVAs of exported symbols.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2711">Il s’agit des adresses réelles des fonctions et des données exportées dans le code exécutable et les sections de données.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2711">These are the actual addresses of the exported functions and data within the executable code and data sections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2712">D’autres fichiers images peuvent importer un symbole à l’aide d’un index de cette table (un ordinal) ou, éventuellement, en utilisant le nom public qui correspond à l’ordinal si un nom public est défini.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2712">Other image files can import a symbol by using an index to this table (an ordinal) or, optionally, by using the public name that corresponds to the ordinal if a public name is defined.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2713">Nom de la table de pointeurs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2713">Name pointer table</span></span> <br/>     | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2714">Tableau de pointeurs vers les noms d’exportation publics, triés dans l’ordre croissant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2714">An array of pointers to the public export names, sorted in ascending order.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2715">Table ordinale</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2715">Ordinal table</span></span> <br/>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2716">Tableau des ordinaux qui correspondent aux membres de la table de pointeurs de nom.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2716">An array of the ordinals that correspond to members of the name pointer table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2717">La correspondance est par position ; par conséquent, la table de pointeurs de nom et la table ordinale doivent avoir le même nombre de membres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2717">The correspondence is by position; therefore, the name pointer table and the ordinal table must have the same number of members.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2718">Chaque ordinal est un index dans la table d’adresses d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2718">Each ordinal is an index into the export address table.</span></span> <br/>                                                                        |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2719">Exporter le nom table</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2719">Export name table</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2720">Une série de chaînes ASCII se terminant par un caractère null.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2720">A series of null-terminated ASCII strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2721">Les membres de la table de pointeur de nom pointent dans cette zone.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2721">Members of the name pointer table point into this area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2722">Ces noms sont les noms publics par le biais desquels les symboles sont importés et exportés ; ils ne sont pas nécessairement les mêmes que les noms privés utilisés dans le fichier image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2722">These names are the public names through which the symbols are imported and exported; they are not necessarily the same as the private names that are used within the image file.</span></span> <br/>                                                           |



 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2723">Lorsqu’un autre fichier image importe un symbole par nom, le chargeur Win32 recherche une chaîne correspondante dans la table de pointeur de nom.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2723">When another image file imports a symbol by name, the Win32 loader searches the name pointer table for a matching string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2724">Si une chaîne correspondante est trouvée, l’ordinal associé est identifié en recherchant le membre correspondant dans la table ordinale (autrement dit, le membre de la table ordinale avec le même index que le pointeur de chaîne trouvé dans la table de pointeur de nom).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2724">If a matching string is found, the associated ordinal is identified by looking up the corresponding member in the ordinal table (that is, the member of the ordinal table with the same index as the string pointer found in the name pointer table).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2725">L’ordinal résultant est un index dans la table d’adresses d’exportation, qui donne l’emplacement réel du symbole souhaité.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2725">The resulting ordinal is an index into the export address table, which gives the actual location of the desired symbol.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2726">Chaque symbole d’exportation est accessible par un ordinal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2726">Every export symbol can be accessed by an ordinal.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2727">Lorsqu’un autre fichier image importe un symbole par ordinal, il n’est pas nécessaire d’effectuer une recherche dans la table de pointeur de nom pour une chaîne correspondante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2727">When another image file imports a symbol by ordinal, it is unnecessary to search the name pointer table for a matching string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2728">L’utilisation directe d’un ordinal est donc plus efficace.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2728">Direct use of an ordinal is therefore more efficient.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2729">Toutefois, un nom d’exportation est plus facile à mémoriser et ne demande pas à l’utilisateur de connaître l’index de table pour le symbole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2729">However, an export name is easier to remember and does not require the user to know the table index for the symbol.</span></span>

#### <a name="export-directory-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2730">Exporter une table de répertoire</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2730">Export Directory Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2731">Les informations sur les symboles d’exportation commencent par la table de répertoire d’exportation, qui décrit le reste des informations de symbole d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2731">The export symbol information begins with the export directory table, which describes the remainder of the export symbol information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2732">La table exporter le répertoire contient des informations d’adresse utilisées pour résoudre les importations des points d’entrée dans cette image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2732">The export directory table contains address information that is used to resolve imports to the entry points within this image.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2750">10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2750">10</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2751">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2751">2</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2752">Version mineure</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2752">Minor Version</span></span> <br/>            | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2753">Numéro de version secondaire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2753">The minor version number.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                     |

| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2759">16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2759">16</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2760">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2760">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2761">Base ordinale</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2761">Ordinal Base</span></span> <br/>             | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2762">Nombre ordinal de départ pour les exportations dans cette image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2762">The starting ordinal number for exports in this image.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2763">Ce champ spécifie le numéro ordinal de début de la table d’adresses d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2763">This field specifies the starting ordinal number for the export address table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2764">Il est généralement défini sur 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2764">It is usually set to 1.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2765">20</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2765">20</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2766">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2766">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2767">Entrées de la table Address</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2767">Address Table Entries</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2768">Nombre d’entrées dans la table d’adresses d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2768">The number of entries in the export address table.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2769">24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2769">24</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2770">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2770">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2771">Nombre de pointeurs de nom</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2771">Number of Name Pointers</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2772">Nombre d’entrées dans la table de pointeurs de nom.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2772">The number of entries in the name pointer table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2773">Il s’agit également du nombre d’entrées dans la table ordinale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2773">This is also the number of entries in the ordinal table.</span></span> <br/>                                                     |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2774">28</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2774">28</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2775">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2775">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2776">Adresse RVA d’exportation de table d’adresses</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2776">Export Address Table RVA</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2777">Adresse de la table d’adresses d’exportation, par rapport à la base de l’image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2777">The address of the export address table, relative to the image base.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                          |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2778">32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2778">32</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2779">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2779">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2780">Nom RVA du pointeur de nom</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2780">Name Pointer RVA</span></span> <br/>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2781">Adresse de la table de pointeurs du nom d’exportation, relative à la base de l’image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2781">The address of the export name pointer table, relative to the image base.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2782">La taille de la table est donnée par le champ nombre de pointeurs de nom.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2782">The table size is given by the Number of Name Pointers field.</span></span> <br/>                       |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2783">36</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2783">36</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2784">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2784">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2785">RVA de table ordinale</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2785">Ordinal Table RVA</span></span> <br/>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2786">Adresse de la table ordinale par rapport à la base de l’image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2786">The address of the ordinal table, relative to the image base.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                 |



 

#### <a name="export-address-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2787">Exporter une table d’adresses</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2787">Export Address Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2788">La table d’adresses d’exportation contient l’adresse des points d’entrée exportés et des données exportées et des données absolues.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2788">The export address table contains the address of exported entry points and exported data and absolutes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2789">Un nombre ordinal est utilisé comme index dans la table d’adresses d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2789">An ordinal number is used as an index into the export address table.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2790">Chaque entrée dans la table d’adresses d’exportation est un champ qui utilise l’un des deux formats figurant dans le tableau suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2790">Each entry in the export address table is a field that uses one of two formats in the following table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2791">Si l’adresse spécifiée n’est pas comprise dans la section d’exportation (comme défini par l’adresse et la longueur indiqués dans l’en-tête facultatif), le champ est un RVA d’exportation, qui est une adresse réelle dans le code ou les données.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2791">If the address specified is not within the export section (as defined by the address and length that are indicated in the optional header), the field is an export RVA, which is an actual address in code or data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2792">Dans le cas contraire, le champ est un RVA de redirecteur, qui nomme un symbole dans une autre DLL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2792">Otherwise, the field is a forwarder RVA, which names a symbol in another DLL.</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2793">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2793">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2794">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2794">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2795">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2795">Field</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2796">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2796">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
|---------------|---------------|---------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2797">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2797">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2798">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2798">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2799">Exporter un RVA</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2799">Export RVA</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2800">Adresse du symbole exporté lorsqu’il est chargé en mémoire, par rapport à la base de l’image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2800">The address of the exported symbol when loaded into memory, relative to the image base.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2801">Par exemple, l’adresse d’une fonction exportée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2801">For example, the address of an exported function.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2802">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2802">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2803">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2803">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2804">RVA du redirecteur</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2804">Forwarder RVA</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2805">Pointeur vers une chaîne ASCII terminée par le caractère NULL dans la section d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2805">The pointer to a null-terminated ASCII string in the export section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2806">Cette chaîne doit être comprise dans la plage fournie par l’entrée de répertoire de données de table d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2806">This string must be within the range that is given by the export table data directory entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2807">Consultez les [répertoires de données d’en-tête facultatifs (image uniquement)](#optional-header-data-directories-image-only).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2807">See [Optional Header Data Directories (Image Only)](#optional-header-data-directories-image-only).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2808">Cette chaîne indique le nom de la DLL et le nom de l’exportation (par exemple, « MYDLL. expfunc ») ou le nom de la DLL et le numéro ordinal de l’exportation (par exemple, «MYDLL. \# 27 ").</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2808">This string gives the DLL name and the name of the export (for example, "MYDLL.expfunc") or the DLL name and the ordinal number of the export (for example, "MYDLL.\#27").</span></span> <br/> |



 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2809">Une adresse RVA de redirecteur exporte une définition à partir d’une autre image, en la faisant apparaître comme si elle était exportée par l’image actuelle.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2809">A forwarder RVA exports a definition from some other image, making it appear as if it were being exported by the current image.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2810">Par conséquent, le symbole est importé et exporté simultanément.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2810">Thus, the symbol is simultaneously imported and exported.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2811">Par exemple, dans Kernel32.dll dans Windows XP, l’exportation nommée « HeapAlloc » est transmise à la chaîne «NTDLL. RtlAllocateHeap."</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2811">For example, in Kernel32.dll in Windows XP, the export named "HeapAlloc" is forwarded to the string "NTDLL.RtlAllocateHeap."</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2812">Cela permet aux applications d’utiliser le module spécifique à Windows XP Ntdll.dll sans réellement contenir des références d’importation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2812">This allows applications to use the Windows XP-specific module Ntdll.dll without actually containing import references to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2813">La table d’importation de l’application fait uniquement référence à Kernel32.dll.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2813">The application's import table refers only to Kernel32.dll.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2814">Par conséquent, l’application n’est pas spécifique à Windows XP et peut s’exécuter sur n’importe quel système Win32.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2814">Therefore, the application is not specific to Windows XP and can run on any Win32 system.</span></span>

#### <a name="export-name-pointer-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2815">Exporter le nom de la table de pointeurs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2815">Export Name Pointer Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2816">La table de pointeurs de nom d’exportation est un tableau d’adresses (RVA) dans la table de noms d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2816">The export name pointer table is an array of addresses (RVAs) into the export name table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2817">Les pointeurs sont 32 bits chacun et sont relatifs à la base de l’image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2817">The pointers are 32 bits each and are relative to the image base.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2818">Les pointeurs sont triés lexicalement pour autoriser les recherches binaires.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2818">The pointers are ordered lexically to allow binary searches.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2819">Un nom d’exportation est défini uniquement si la table du pointeur de nom d’exportation contient un pointeur vers celui-ci.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2819">An export name is defined only if the export name pointer table contains a pointer to it.</span></span>

#### <a name="export-ordinal-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2820">Exporter une table ordinale</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2820">Export Ordinal Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2821">La table ordinale d’exportation est un tableau d’index non biaisés 16 bits dans la table d’adresses d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2821">The export ordinal table is an array of 16-bit unbiased indexes into the export address table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2822">Les ordinaux sont faussés par le champ de base ordinal de la table de répertoire d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2822">Ordinals are biased by the Ordinal Base field of the export directory table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2823">En d’autres termes, la base ordinale doit être soustraite des ordinaux pour obtenir les véritables index dans la table d’adresses d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2823">In other words, the ordinal base must be subtracted from the ordinals to obtain true indexes into the export address table.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2824">La table du pointeur de nom d’exportation et la table ordinale d’exportation forment deux tableaux parallèles séparés pour permettre l’alignement de champ naturel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2824">The export name pointer table and the export ordinal table form two parallel arrays that are separated to allow natural field alignment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2825">Ces deux tables, en effet, fonctionnent comme une seule table, dans laquelle la colonne de pointeur de nom d’exportation pointe vers un nom public (exporté) et la colonne d’ordinal d’exportation donne l’ordinal correspondant pour ce nom public.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2825">These two tables, in effect, operate as one table, in which the Export Name Pointer column points to a public (exported) name and the Export Ordinal column gives the corresponding ordinal for that public name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2826">Un membre de la table de pointeurs de nom d’exportation et un membre de la table ordinale d’exportation sont associés à la même position (index) dans leurs tableaux respectifs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2826">A member of the export name pointer table and a member of the export ordinal table are associated by having the same position (index) in their respective arrays.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2827">Ainsi, lorsque la table de pointeurs de nom d’exportation est recherchée et qu’une chaîne correspondante est trouvée à la position i, l’algorithme de recherche des RVA du symbole et de l’ordinal biaisé est le suivant :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2827">Thus, when the export name pointer table is searched and a matching string is found at position i, the algorithm for finding the symbol's RVA and biased ordinal is:</span></span>

```C++
i = Search_ExportNamePointerTable (name);
ordinal = ExportOrdinalTable [i];

rva = ExportAddressTable [ordinal];
biased_ordinal = ordinal + OrdinalBase;
```

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2828">Lors de la recherche d’un symbole (biais) ordinal, l’algorithme permettant de trouver l’adresse RVA du symbole et le nom est :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2828">When searching for a symbol by (biased) ordinal, the algorithm for finding the symbol's RVA and name is:</span></span>

```C++
ordinal = biased_ordinal - OrdinalBase;
i = Search_ExportOrdinalTable (ordinal);

rva = ExportAddressTable [ordinal];
name = ExportNameTable [i];
```

#### <a name="export-name-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2829">Exporter le nom table</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2829">Export Name Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2830">La table nom d’exportation contient les données de chaîne réelles pointées par la table du pointeur de nom d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2830">The export name table contains the actual string data that was pointed to by the export name pointer table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2831">Les chaînes de cette table sont des noms publics que d’autres images peuvent utiliser pour importer les symboles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2831">The strings in this table are public names that other images can use to import the symbols.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2832">Ces noms d’exportation publics ne sont pas nécessairement les mêmes que les noms de symboles privés dont disposent les symboles dans leur propre fichier image et code source, bien qu’ils puissent l’être.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2832">These public export names are not necessarily the same as the private symbol names that the symbols have in their own image file and source code, although they can be.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2833">Chaque symbole exporté a une valeur ordinale, qui est simplement l’index dans la table d’adresses d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2833">Every exported symbol has an ordinal value, which is just the index into the export address table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2834">Toutefois, l’utilisation de noms d’exportation est facultative.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2834">Use of export names, however, is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2835">Tout, tout ou aucun des symboles exportés peut avoir des noms d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2835">Some, all, or none of the exported symbols can have export names.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2836">Pour les symboles exportés qui ont des noms d’exportation, les entrées correspondantes dans la table de pointeur de nom d’exportation et la table ordinale d’exportation fonctionnent ensemble pour associer chaque nom à un ordinal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2836">For exported symbols that do have export names, corresponding entries in the export name pointer table and export ordinal table work together to associate each name with an ordinal.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2837">La structure de la table de noms d’exportation est une série de chaînes ASCII se terminant par un caractère null de longueur variable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2837">The structure of the export name table is a series of null-terminated ASCII strings of variable length.</span></span>

### <a name="the-idata-section"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2838">Section. idata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2838">The .idata Section</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2839">Tous les fichiers image qui importent des symboles, y compris pratiquement tous les fichiers exécutables (EXE), ont une section. idata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2839">All image files that import symbols, including virtually all executable (EXE) files, have an .idata section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2840">Une mise en page de fichier standard pour les informations d’importation est la suivante :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2840">A typical file layout for the import information follows:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2841">Table de répertoire</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2841">Directory Table</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2842">Entrée de répertoire null</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2842">Null Directory Entry</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2843">DLL1 importer la table de recherche</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2843">DLL1 Import Lookup Table</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2844">Null</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2844">Null</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2845">DLL2 importer la table de recherche</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2845">DLL2 Import Lookup Table</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2846">Null</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2846">Null</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2847">DLL3 importer la table de recherche</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2847">DLL3 Import Lookup Table</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2848">Null</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2848">Null</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2849">Table Hint-Name</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2849">Hint-Name Table</span></span>

#### <a name="import-directory-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2850">Importer une table de répertoire</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2850">Import Directory Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2851">Les informations d’importation commencent par la table d’importation des répertoires, qui décrit le reste des informations d’importation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2851">The import information begins with the import directory table, which describes the remainder of the import information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2852">La table du répertoire d’importation contient des informations d’adresse utilisées pour résoudre les références de correction aux points d’entrée dans une image DLL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2852">The import directory table contains address information that is used to resolve fixup references to the entry points within a DLL image.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2853">La table d’importation des répertoires se compose d’un tableau d’entrées de répertoire d’importation, d’une entrée pour chaque DLL à laquelle l’image fait référence.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2853">The import directory table consists of an array of import directory entries, one entry for each DLL to which the image refers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2854">La dernière entrée de répertoire est vide (remplie avec des valeurs null), ce qui indique la fin de la table de répertoires.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2854">The last directory entry is empty (filled with null values), which indicates the end of the directory table.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2855">Chaque entrée de répertoire d’importation a le format suivant :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2855">Each import directory entry has the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2856">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2856">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2857">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2857">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2858">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2858">Field</span></span>                                                 | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2859">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2859">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                 |
|----------------|---------------|-------------------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2860">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2860">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2861">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2861">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2862">Importer les RVA de table de recherche (caractéristiques)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2862">Import Lookup Table RVA (Characteristics)</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2863">Adresse RVA de la table de recherche d’importation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2863">The RVA of the import lookup table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2864">Cette table contient un nom ou un ordinal pour chaque importation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2864">This table contains a name or ordinal for each import.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2865">(Le nom « caractéristiques » est utilisé dans Winnt. h, mais ne décrit plus ce champ.)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2865">(The name "Characteristics" is used in Winnt.h, but no longer describes this field.)</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2866">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2866">4</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2867">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2867">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2868">Horodatage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2868">Time/Date Stamp</span></span> <br/>                           | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2869">Horodatage défini à zéro jusqu’à ce que l’image soit liée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2869">The stamp that is set to zero until the image is bound.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2870">Une fois l’image liée, ce champ a pour valeur l’horodatage de la DLL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2870">After the image is bound, this field is set to the time/data stamp of the DLL.</span></span> <br/>                                          |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2871">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2871">8</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2872">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2872">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2873">Chaîne de redirecteur</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2873">Forwarder Chain</span></span> <br/>                           | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2874">Index de la première référence de redirecteur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2874">The index of the first forwarder reference.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                     |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2875">12</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2875">12</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2876">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2876">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2877">Nom RVA</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2877">Name RVA</span></span> <br/>                                  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2878">Adresse d’une chaîne ASCII qui contient le nom de la DLL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2878">The address of an ASCII string that contains the name of the DLL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2879">Cette adresse est relative à la base de l’image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2879">This address is relative to the image base.</span></span> <br/>                                                                   |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2880">16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2880">16</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2881">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2881">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2882">Importer une adresse RVA de table d’adresses (table thunk)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2882">Import Address Table RVA (Thunk Table)</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2883">Adresse RVA de la table d’adresses d’importation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2883">The RVA of the import address table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2884">Le contenu de cette table est identique au contenu de la table de recherche d’importation jusqu’à ce que l’image soit liée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2884">The contents of this table are identical to the contents of the import lookup table until the image is bound.</span></span> <br/>                              |



 

#### <a name="import-lookup-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2885">Importer une table de recherche</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2885">Import Lookup Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2886">Une table de recherche d’importation est un tableau de nombres 32 bits pour PE32 ou un tableau de nombres 64 bits pour PE32 +.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2886">An import lookup table is an array of 32-bit numbers for PE32 or an array of 64-bit numbers for PE32+.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2887">Chaque entrée utilise le format de champ de bits qui est décrit dans le tableau suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2887">Each entry uses the bit-field format that is described in the following table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2888">Dans ce format, le bit 31 est le bit le plus significatif pour PE32 et le bit 63 est le bit le plus significatif pour PE32 +.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2888">In this format, bit 31 is the most significant bit for PE32 and bit 63 is the most significant bit for PE32+.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2889">La collection de ces entrées décrit toutes les importations à partir d’une DLL donnée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2889">The collection of these entries describes all imports from a given DLL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2890">La dernière entrée est définie sur zéro (NULL) pour indiquer la fin de la table.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2890">The last entry is set to zero (NULL) to indicate the end of the table.</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2891">Bit (s)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2891">Bit(s)</span></span>            | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2892">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2892">Size</span></span>           | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2893">Champ de bits</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2893">Bit field</span></span>                       | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2894">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2894">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                               |
|-------------------|----------------|---------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2895">31/63</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2895">31/63</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2896">1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2896">1</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2897">Indicateur de nom/ordinal</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2897">Ordinal/Name Flag</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2898">Si ce bit est défini, importez par ordinal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2898">If this bit is set, import by ordinal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2899">Dans le cas contraire, importez par nom.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2899">Otherwise, import by name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2900">Le bit est masqué en 0x80000000 pour PE32, 0x8000000000000000 pour PE32 +.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2900">Bit is masked as 0x80000000 for PE32, 0x8000000000000000 for PE32+.</span></span> <br/>                         |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2901">15-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2901">15-0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2902">16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2902">16</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2903">Nombre ordinal</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2903">Ordinal Number</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2904">Nombre ordinal de 16 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2904">A 16-bit ordinal number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2905">Ce champ est utilisé uniquement si le champ de bits de l’indicateur ordinal/nom est 1 (importer par ordinal).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2905">This field is used only if the Ordinal/Name Flag bit field is 1 (import by ordinal).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2906">Les bits 30-15 ou 62-15 doivent avoir la valeur 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2906">Bits 30-15 or 62-15 must be 0.</span></span> <br/>                  |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2907">30-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2907">30-0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2908">31</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2908">31</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2909">Adresse RVA/nom de la table RVA</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2909">Hint/Name Table RVA</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2910">RVA de 31 bits d’une entrée de table Hint/Name.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2910">A 31-bit RVA of a hint/name table entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2911">Ce champ est utilisé uniquement si le champ de bits de l’indicateur ordinal/nom a la valeur 0 (importer par nom).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2911">This field is used only if the Ordinal/Name Flag bit field is 0 (import by name).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2912">Pour PE32 + bits 62-31 doit être égal à zéro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2912">For PE32+ bits 62-31 must be zero.</span></span> <br/> |



 

#### <a name="hintname-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2913">Table Hint/Name</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2913">Hint/Name Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2914">Une table Hint/Name est suffisante pour l’intégralité de la section Import.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2914">One hint/name table suffices for the entire import section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2915">Chaque entrée dans la table Hint/Name a le format suivant :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2915">Each entry in the hint/name table has the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2916">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2916">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2917">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2917">Size</span></span>                 | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2918">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2918">Field</span></span>            | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2919">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2919">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                       |
|----------------|----------------------|------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2920">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2920">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2921">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2921">2</span></span> <br/>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2922">Évit</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2922">Hint</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2923">Index dans la table de pointeurs de nom d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2923">An index into the export name pointer table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2924">Une correspondance est tentée en premier avec cette valeur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2924">A match is attempted first with this value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2925">En cas d’échec, une recherche binaire est effectuée sur la table du pointeur de nom d’exportation de la DLL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2925">If it fails, a binary search is performed on the DLL's export name pointer table.</span></span> <br/>            |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2926">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2926">2</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2927">variable</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2927">variable</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2928">Nom</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2928">Name</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2929">Chaîne ASCII qui contient le nom à importer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2929">An ASCII string that contains the name to import.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2930">Il s’agit de la chaîne qui doit être mise en correspondance avec le nom public dans la DLL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2930">This is the string that must be matched to the public name in the DLL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2931">Cette chaîne respecte la casse et se termine par un octet NULL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2931">This string is case sensitive and terminated by a null byte.</span></span> <br/> |
| \* <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2932">0 ou 1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2932">0 or 1</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2933">Remplir</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2933">Pad</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2934">Octet de remplissage zéro à droite qui apparaît après l’octet NULL de fin, si nécessaire, pour aligner l’entrée suivante sur une limite égale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2934">A trailing zero-pad byte that appears after the trailing null byte, if necessary, to align the next entry on an even boundary.</span></span> <br/>                                                        |



 

#### <a name="import-address-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2935">Table d’adresses d’importation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2935">Import Address Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2936">La structure et le contenu de la table d’adresses d’importation sont identiques à ceux de la table de recherche d’importation, jusqu’à ce que le fichier soit lié.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2936">The structure and content of the import address table are identical to those of the import lookup table, until the file is bound.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2937">Pendant la liaison, les entrées de la table d’adresses d’importation sont remplacées par les adresses 32 bits (pour PE32) ou 64 bits (pour PE32 +) des symboles en cours d’importation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2937">During binding, the entries in the import address table are overwritten with the 32-bit (for PE32) or 64-bit (for PE32+) addresses of the symbols that are being imported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2938">Ces adresses sont les adresses mémoire réelles des symboles, bien qu’elles soient techniquement appelées « adresses virtuelles ».</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2938">These addresses are the actual memory addresses of the symbols, although technically they are still called "virtual addresses."</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2939">Le chargeur traite généralement la liaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2939">The loader typically processes the binding.</span></span>

### <a name="the-pdata-section"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-2940">La section. pdata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2940">The .pdata Section</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2941">La section. pData contient un tableau d’entrées de table de fonctions utilisées pour la gestion des exceptions.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2941">The .pdata section contains an array of function table entries that are used for exception handling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2942">Elle est référencée par l’entrée de la table d’exceptions dans le répertoire de données de l’image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2942">It is pointed to by the exception table entry in the image data directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2943">Les entrées doivent être triées en fonction des adresses des fonctions (le premier champ de chaque structure) avant d’être émises dans l’image finale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2943">The entries must be sorted according to the function addresses (the first field in each structure) before being emitted into the final image.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2944">La plateforme cible détermine laquelle des trois variantes de format d’entrée de table de fonction décrites ci-dessous est utilisée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2944">The target platform determines which of the three function table entry format variations described below is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2945">Pour les images MIPS 32 bits, les entrées de la table de fonctions ont le format suivant :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2945">For 32-bit MIPS images, function table entries have the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2946">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2946">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2947">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2947">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2948">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2948">Field</span></span>                          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2949">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2949">Description</span></span>                                                                    |
|----------------|---------------|--------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
