| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2950">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2950">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2951">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2951">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2952">Adresse de début</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2952">Begin Address</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2953">VA de la fonction correspondante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2953">The VA of the corresponding function.</span></span> <br/>                              |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2954">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2954">4</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2955">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2955">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2956">Adresse de fin</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2956">End Address</span></span> <br/>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2957">VA de la fin de la fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2957">The VA of the end of the function.</span></span> <br/>                                 |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2958">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2958">8</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2959">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2959">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2960">Gestionnaire d’exceptions</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2960">Exception Handler</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2961">Pointeur vers le gestionnaire d’exceptions à exécuter.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2961">The pointer to the exception handler to be executed.</span></span> <br/>               |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2962">12</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2962">12</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2963">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2963">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2964">Données du gestionnaire</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2964">Handler Data</span></span> <br/>       | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2965">Pointeur vers des informations supplémentaires à passer au gestionnaire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2965">The pointer to additional information to be passed to the handler.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2966">16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2966">16</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2967">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2967">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2968">Adresse de fin du prologue</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2968">Prolog End Address</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2969">VA de la fin du prologue de la fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2969">The VA of the end of the function's prolog.</span></span> <br/>                        |



 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2970">Pour les plateformes ARM, PowerPC, SH3 et SH4 Windows CE, les entrées de la table de fonctions ont le format suivant :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2970">For the ARM, PowerPC, SH3 and SH4 Windows CE platforms, function table entries have the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2971">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2971">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2972">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2972">Size</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2973">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2973">Field</span></span>                       | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2974">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2974">Description</span></span>                                                                                                               |
|---------------|---------------------|-----------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2975">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2975">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2976">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2976">4</span></span> <br/>       | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2977">Adresse de début</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2977">Begin Address</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2978">VA de la fonction correspondante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2978">The VA of the corresponding function.</span></span> <br/>                                                                         |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2979">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2979">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2980">8 bits</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2980">8 bits</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2981">Longueur du prologue</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2981">Prolog Length</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2982">Nombre d’instructions dans le prologue de la fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2982">The number of instructions in the function's prolog.</span></span> <br/>                                                          |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2983">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2983">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2984">22 bits</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2984">22 bits</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2985">Longueur de la fonction</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2985">Function Length</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2986">Nombre d’instructions dans la fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2986">The number of instructions in the function.</span></span> <br/>                                                                   |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2987">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2987">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2988">1 bit</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2988">1 bit</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2989">Indicateur 32 bits</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2989">32-bit Flag</span></span> <br/>     | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2990">Si cette valeur est définie, la fonction se compose d’instructions 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2990">If set, the function consists of 32-bit instructions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2991">Si elle est désactivée, la fonction se compose d’instructions 16 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2991">If clear, the function consists of 16-bit instructions.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2992">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2992">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2993">1 bit</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2993">1 bit</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2994">Indicateur d’exception</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2994">Exception Flag</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2995">S’il est défini, il existe un gestionnaire d’exceptions pour la fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2995">If set, an exception handler exists for the function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2996">Sinon, il n’existe aucun gestionnaire d’exceptions.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2996">Otherwise, no exception handler exists.</span></span> <br/>                 |



 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-2997">Pour les plateformes x64 et Itanium, les entrées de table de fonctions ont le format suivant :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2997">For x64 and Itanium platforms, function table entries have the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2998">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2998">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-2999">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-2999">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3000">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3000">Field</span></span>                          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3001">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3001">Description</span></span>                                        |
|---------------|---------------|--------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3002">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3002">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3003">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3003">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3004">Adresse de début</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3004">Begin Address</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3005">RVA de la fonction correspondante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3005">The RVA of the corresponding function.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3006">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3006">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3007">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3007">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3008">Adresse de fin</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3008">End Address</span></span> <br/>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3009">RVA de la fin de la fonction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3009">The RVA of the end of the function.</span></span> <br/>    |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3010">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3010">8</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3011">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3011">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3012">Informations de déroulement</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3012">Unwind Information</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3013">Adresse RVA des informations de déroulement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3013">The RVA of the unwind information.</span></span> <br/>     |



 

### <a name="the-reloc-section-image-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3014">Section. reloc (image uniquement)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3014">The .reloc Section (Image Only)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3015">La table de réadressage de base contient des entrées pour toutes les réadressages de base dans l’image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3015">The base relocation table contains entries for all base relocations in the image.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3016">Le champ de table de réadressage de base dans les répertoires de données d’en-tête facultatifs indique le nombre d’octets dans la table de réadressage de base.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3016">The Base Relocation Table field in the optional header data directories gives the number of bytes in the base relocation table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3017">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [répertoires de données d’en-tête facultatifs (image uniquement)](#optional-header-data-directories-image-only).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3017">For more information, see [Optional Header Data Directories (Image Only)](#optional-header-data-directories-image-only).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3018">La table de réadressage de base est divisée en blocs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3018">The base relocation table is divided into blocks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3019">Chaque bloc représente les réadressages de base pour une page 4K.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3019">Each block represents the base relocations for a 4K page.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3020">Chaque bloc doit démarrer sur une limite de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3020">Each block must start on a 32-bit boundary.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3021">Le chargeur n’est pas requis pour traiter les réadressages de base résolus par l’éditeur de liens, sauf si l’image de chargement ne peut pas être chargée au niveau de la base d’image spécifiée dans l’en-tête PE.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3021">The loader is not required to process base relocations that are resolved by the linker, unless the load image cannot be loaded at the image base that is specified in the PE header.</span></span>

#### <a name="base-relocation-block"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3022">Bloc de réadressage de base</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3022">Base Relocation Block</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3023">Chaque bloc de réadressage de base commence par la structure suivante :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3023">Each base relocation block starts with the following structure:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3024">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3024">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3025">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3025">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3026">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3026">Field</span></span>                  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3027">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3027">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                              |
|---------------|---------------|------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3028">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3028">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3029">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3029">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3030">RVA de page</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3030">Page RVA</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3031">La base de l’image plus l’adresse RVA de la page est ajoutée à chaque décalage pour créer le VA où le réadressage de base doit être appliqué.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3031">The image base plus the page RVA is added to each offset to create the VA where the base relocation must be applied.</span></span> <br/>                         |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3032">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3032">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3033">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3033">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3034">Taille de bloc</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3034">Block Size</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3035">Nombre total d’octets dans le bloc de réadressage de base, y compris les champs de la page RVA et de la taille de bloc, ainsi que les champs de type/décalage qui suivent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3035">The total number of bytes in the base relocation block, including the Page RVA and Block Size fields and the Type/Offset fields that follow.</span></span> <br/> |



 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3036">Le champ Taille de bloc est alors suivi de n’importe quel nombre d’entrées de champ de type ou de décalage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3036">The Block Size field is then followed by any number of Type or Offset field entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3037">Chaque entrée est un mot (2 octets) et sa structure est la suivante :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3037">Each entry is a WORD (2 bytes) and has the following structure:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3038">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3038">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3039">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3039">Size</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3040">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3040">Field</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3041">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3041">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                            |
|---------------|---------------------|--------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3042">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3042">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3043">4 bits</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3043">4 bits</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3044">Type</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3044">Type</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3045">Stocké dans les 4 bits de poids fort du mot, valeur qui indique le type de réadressage de base à appliquer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3045">Stored in the high 4 bits of the WORD, a value that indicates the type of base relocation to be applied.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3046">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [types de réadressage de base](#base-relocation-types).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3046">For more information, see [Base Relocation Types](#base-relocation-types).</span></span><br/>                         |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3047">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3047">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3048">12 bits</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3048">12 bits</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3049">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3049">Offset</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3050">Stocké dans les 12 bits restants du mot, décalage par rapport à l’adresse de départ spécifiée dans le champ de la page RVA du bloc.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3050">Stored in the remaining 12 bits of the WORD, an offset from the starting address that was specified in the Page RVA field for the block.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3051">Ce décalage spécifie où le réadressage de base doit être appliqué.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3051">This offset specifies where the base relocation is to be applied.</span></span> <br/> |



 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3052">Pour appliquer un réadressage de base, la différence est calculée entre l’adresse de base préférée et la base dans laquelle l’image est réellement chargée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3052">To apply a base relocation, the difference is calculated between the preferred base address and the base where the image is actually loaded.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3053">Si l’image est chargée à sa base par défaut, la différence est égale à zéro et les réadressages de base ne doivent donc pas être appliqués.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3053">If the image is loaded at its preferred base, the difference is zero and thus the base relocations do not have to be applied.</span></span>

#### <a name="base-relocation-types"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3054">Types de réadressage de base</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3054">Base Relocation Types</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3055">Constante</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3055">Constant</span></span>                                       | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3056">Valeur</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3056">Value</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3057">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3057">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
|------------------------------------------------|----------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3058">IMAGE \_ \_ basée sur une rel. \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3058">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_ABSOLUTE</span></span> <br/>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3059">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3059">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3060">Le réadressage de base est ignoré.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3060">The base relocation is skipped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3061">Ce type peut être utilisé pour remplir un bloc.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3061">This type can be used to pad a block.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3062">IMAGE \_ rel \_ basée sur la \_ hauteur</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3062">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_HIGH</span></span> <br/>            | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3063">1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3063">1</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3064">Le réadressage de base ajoute les 16 bits de poids fort de la différence au champ de 16 bits au décalage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3064">The base relocation adds the high 16 bits of the difference to the 16-bit field at offset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3065">Le champ de 16 bits représente la valeur élevée d’un mot de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3065">The 16-bit field represents the high value of a 32-bit word.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                               |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3066">base d’IMAGE \_ rel \_ \_ faible</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3066">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_LOW</span></span> <br/>             | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3067">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3067">2</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3068">Le réadressage de base ajoute les 16 bits de poids faible de la différence au champ de 16 bits au décalage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3068">The base relocation adds the low 16 bits of the difference to the 16-bit field at offset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3069">Le champ de 16 bits représente la moitié inférieure d’un mot de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3069">The 16-bit field represents the low half of a 32-bit word.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                  |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3070">\_ \_ HIGHLOW basé sur une image \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3070">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_HIGHLOW</span></span> <br/>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3071">3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3071">3</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3072">Le réadressage de base applique tous les 32 bits de la différence au champ de 32 bits au décalage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3072">The base relocation applies all 32 bits of the difference to the 32-bit field at offset.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3073">\_ \_ HIGHADJ basé sur une image \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3073">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_HIGHADJ</span></span> <br/>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3074">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3074">4</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3075">Le réadressage de base ajoute les 16 bits de poids fort de la différence au champ de 16 bits au décalage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3075">The base relocation adds the high 16 bits of the difference to the 16-bit field at offset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3076">Le champ de 16 bits représente la valeur élevée d’un mot de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3076">The 16-bit field represents the high value of a 32-bit word.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3077">Les 16 bits de poids faible de la valeur 32 bits sont stockés dans le mot 16 bits qui suit ce réadressage de base.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3077">The low 16 bits of the 32-bit value are stored in the 16-bit word that follows this base relocation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3078">Cela signifie que ce réadressage de base occupe deux emplacements.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3078">This means that this base relocation occupies two slots.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3079">\_JMPADDR des \_ mips basés sur une \_ image \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3079">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_MIPS\_JMPADDR</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3080">5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3080">5</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3081">L’interprétation du réadressage dépend du type d’ordinateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3081">The relocation interpretation is dependent on the machine type.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3082">Lorsque le type d’ordinateur est MIPS, le réadressage de base s’applique à une instruction de saut MIPS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3082">When the machine type is MIPS, the base relocation applies to a MIPS jump instruction.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                    |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3083">IMAGE \_ \_ MOV32 ARM basé sur une rel. \_ \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3083">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_ARM\_MOV32</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3084">5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3084">5</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3085">Ce déplacement est significatif uniquement lorsque le type d’ordinateur est ARM ou Thumb.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3085">This relocation is meaningful only when the machine type is ARM or Thumb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3086">Le réadressage de base applique l’adresse 32 bits d’un symbole sur une paire d’instructions MOVW/MOVT consécutive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3086">The base relocation applies the 32-bit address of a symbol across a consecutive MOVW/MOVT instruction pair.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                 |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3087">\_ \_ \_ RISCV HIGH20 basé sur \_ une image</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3087">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_RISCV\_HIGH20</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3088">5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3088">5</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3089">Ce déplacement est significatif uniquement lorsque le type d’ordinateur est RISC-V.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3089">This relocation is only meaningful when the machine type is RISC-V.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3090">Le réadressage de base s’applique aux 20 bits de poids fort d’une adresse absolue de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3090">The base relocation applies to the high 20 bits of a 32-bit absolute address.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                     |
|                                                | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3091">6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3091">6</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3092">Réservé, doit être égal à zéro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3092">Reserved, must be zero.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                               |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3093">\_ \_ \_ MOV32 Thumb basé sur \_ une image rel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3093">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_THUMB\_MOV32</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3094">7</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3094">7</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3095">Ce déplacement est significatif uniquement lorsque le type d’ordinateur est Thumb.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3095">This relocation is meaningful only when the machine type is Thumb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3096">Le réadressage de base applique l’adresse 32 bits d’un symbole à une paire d’instructions MOVW/MOVT consécutive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3096">The base relocation applies the 32-bit address of a symbol to a consecutive MOVW/MOVT instruction pair.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3097">\_ \_ \_ RISCV LOW12I basé sur \_ une image</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3097">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_RISCV\_LOW12I</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3098">7</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3098">7</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3099">Ce déplacement est significatif uniquement lorsque le type d’ordinateur est RISC-V.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3099">This relocation is only meaningful when the machine type is RISC-V.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3100">Le réadressage de base s’applique aux 12 bits de poids faible d’une adresse absolue 32 bits formée dans le format d’instruction de type I RISC-V.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3100">The base relocation applies to the low 12 bits of a 32-bit absolute address formed in RISC-V I-type instruction format.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                           |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3101">\_ \_ \_ RISCV LOW12S basé sur \_ une image</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3101">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_RISCV\_LOW12S</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3102">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3102">8</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3103">Ce déplacement est significatif uniquement lorsque le type d’ordinateur est RISC-V.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3103">This relocation is only meaningful when the machine type is RISC-V.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3104">Le réadressage de base s’applique aux 12 bits de poids faible d’une adresse absolue de 32 bits formée dans le format d’instruction de type S RISC-V.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3104">The base relocation applies to the low 12 bits of a 32-bit absolute address formed in RISC-V S-type instruction format.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                           |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3105">\_JMPADDR16 des \_ mips basés sur une \_ image \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3105">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_MIPS\_JMPADDR16</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3106">9</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3106">9</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3107">Le déplacement est significatif uniquement lorsque le type d’ordinateur est MIPS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3107">The relocation is only meaningful when the machine type is MIPS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3108">Le réadressage de base s’applique à une instruction de saut MIPS16.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3108">The base relocation applies to a MIPS16 jump instruction.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3109">\_ \_ DIR64 basé sur une image \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3109">IMAGE\_REL\_BASED\_DIR64</span></span> <br/>           | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3110">10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3110">10</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3111">Le réadressage de base applique la différence au champ de bits 64 au décalage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3111">The base relocation applies the difference to the 64-bit field at offset.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                             |



 

### <a name="the-tls-section"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3112">Section. TLS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3112">The .tls Section</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3113">La section. TLS fournit la prise en charge directe de PE et de COFF pour le stockage local des threads (TLS) statique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3113">The .tls section provides direct PE and COFF support for static thread local storage (TLS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3114">TLS est une classe de stockage spéciale que Windows prend en charge, dans laquelle un objet de données n’est pas une variable automatique (pile), mais est local pour chaque thread qui exécute le code.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3114">TLS is a special storage class that Windows supports in which a data object is not an automatic (stack) variable, yet is local to each individual thread that runs the code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3115">Ainsi, chaque thread peut conserver une valeur différente pour une variable déclarée à l’aide de TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3115">Thus, each thread can maintain a different value for a variable declared by using TLS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3116">Notez que toute quantité de données TLS peut être prise en charge à l’aide des appels d’API TlsAlloc, TlsFree, TlsSetValue et TlsGetValue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3116">Note that any amount of TLS data can be supported by using the API calls TlsAlloc, TlsFree, TlsSetValue, and TlsGetValue.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3117">L’implémentation PE ou COFF est une approche alternative à l’utilisation de l’API et présente l’avantage d’être plus simple du point de vue du programmeur de langage de haut niveau.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3117">The PE or COFF implementation is an alternative approach to using the API and has the advantage of being simpler from the high-level-language programmer's viewpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3118">Cette implémentation permet de définir et d’initialiser les données TLS de la même façon que les variables statiques ordinaires dans un programme.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3118">This implementation enables TLS data to be defined and initialized similarly to ordinary static variables in a program.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3119">Par exemple, dans Visual C++, une variable TLS statique peut être définie comme suit, sans utiliser l’API Windows :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3119">For example, in Visual C++, a static TLS variable can be defined as follows, without using the Windows API:</span></span>

`__declspec (thread) int tlsFlag = 1;`

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3120">Pour prendre en charge cette construction de programmation, la section PE et COFF. TLS spécifie les informations suivantes : les données d’initialisation, les routines de rappel pour l’initialisation et l’arrêt par thread, et l’index TLS, qui sont expliqués dans la discussion suivante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3120">To support this programming construct, the PE and COFF .tls section specifies the following information: initialization data, callback routines for per-thread initialization and termination, and the TLS index, which are explained in the following discussion.</span></span>

> [!Note]
>
> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3121">Les objets de données TLS déclarés statiquement peuvent être utilisés uniquement dans des fichiers image chargés statiquement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3121">Statically declared TLS data objects can be used only in statically loaded image files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3122">En effet, il n’est pas fiable d’utiliser des données TLS statiques dans une DLL, sauf si vous savez que la DLL, ou quelque chose qui lui est lié de manière statique, ne sera jamais chargée de manière dynamique avec la fonction de l’API LoadLibrary.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3122">This fact makes it unreliable to use static TLS data in a DLL unless you know that the DLL, or anything statically linked with it, will never be loaded dynamically with the LoadLibrary API function.</span></span>

 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3123">Le code exécutable accède à un objet de données TLS statique en procédant comme suit :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3123">Executable code accesses a static TLS data object through the following steps:</span></span>

1.  <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3124">Au moment de la liaison, l’éditeur de liens définit l’adresse du champ d’index du répertoire TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3124">At link time, the linker sets the Address of Index field of the TLS directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3125">Ce champ pointe vers un emplacement où le programme s’attend à recevoir l’index TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3125">This field points to a location where the program expects to receive the TLS index.</span></span>

    <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3126">La bibliothèque Runtime de Microsoft facilite ce processus en définissant une image mémoire du répertoire TLS et en lui attribuant le nom spécial « \_ \_ TLS \_ utilisé » (plates-formes Intel x86) ou « \_ TLS \_ utilisé » (autres plateformes).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3126">The Microsoft run-time library facilitates this process by defining a memory image of the TLS directory and giving it the special name "\_\_tls\_used" (Intel x86 platforms) or "\_tls\_used" (other platforms).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3127">L’éditeur de liens recherche cette image mémoire et y utilise les données pour créer le répertoire TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3127">The linker looks for this memory image and uses the data there to create the TLS directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3128">Les autres compilateurs qui prennent en charge TLS et qui fonctionnent avec l’éditeur de liens Microsoft doivent utiliser cette même technique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3128">Other compilers that support TLS and work with the Microsoft linker must use this same technique.</span></span>

2.  <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3129">Quand un thread est créé, le chargeur communique l’adresse du tableau TLS du thread en plaçant l’adresse du bloc d’environnement de thread (TEB) dans le registre FS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3129">When a thread is created, the loader communicates the address of the thread's TLS array by placing the address of the thread environment block (TEB) in the FS register.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3130">Un pointeur vers le tableau TLS se trouve au décalage de 0x2C à partir du début de TEB.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3130">A pointer to the TLS array is at the offset of 0x2C from the beginning of TEB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3131">Ce comportement est spécifique à Intel x86.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3131">This behavior is Intel x86-specific.</span></span>

3.  <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3132">Le chargeur affecte la valeur de l’index TLS à l’emplacement indiqué par l’adresse du champ d’index.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3132">The loader assigns the value of the TLS index to the place that was indicated by the Address of Index field.</span></span>

4.  <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3133">Le code exécutable récupère l’index TLS et également l’emplacement du tableau TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3133">The executable code retrieves the TLS index and also the location of the TLS array.</span></span>

5.  <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3134">Le code utilise l’index TLS et l’emplacement du tableau TLS (en multipliant l’index par 4 et en l’utilisant comme décalage du tableau) pour obtenir l’adresse de la zone de données TLS pour le programme et le module donnés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3134">The code uses the TLS index and the TLS array location (multiplying the index by 4 and using it as an offset to the array) to get the address of the TLS data area for the given program and module.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3135">Chaque thread possède sa propre zone de données TLS, mais cela est transparent pour le programme, ce qui n’a pas besoin de savoir comment les données sont allouées pour des threads individuels.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3135">Each thread has its own TLS data area, but this is transparent to the program, which does not need to know how data is allocated for individual threads.</span></span>

6.  <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3136">Un objet de données TLS individuel est accessible en tant qu’offset fixe dans la zone de données TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3136">An individual TLS data object is accessed as some fixed offset into the TLS data area.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3137">Le tableau TLS est un tableau d’adresses géré par le système pour chaque thread.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3137">The TLS array is an array of addresses that the system maintains for each thread.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3138">Chaque adresse de ce tableau indique l’emplacement des données TLS pour un module donné (EXE ou DLL) dans le programme.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3138">Each address in this array gives the location of TLS data for a given module (EXE or DLL) within the program.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3139">L’index TLS indique le membre du groupe à utiliser.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3139">The TLS index indicates which member of the array to use.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3140">L’index est un nombre (significatif uniquement pour le système) qui identifie le module.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3140">The index is a number (meaningful only to the system) that identifies the module.</span></span>

#### <a name="the-tls-directory"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3141">Le répertoire TLS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3141">The TLS Directory</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3142">Le répertoire TLS a le format suivant :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3142">The TLS directory has the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3143">Décalage (PE32/PE32 +)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3143">Offset (PE32/ PE32+)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3144">Taille (PE32/PE32 +)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3144">Size (PE32/ PE32+)</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3145">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3145">Field</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3146">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3146">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                         |
|----------------------|--------------------|----------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3147">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3147">0</span></span> <br/>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3148">4/8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3148">4/8</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3149">VA démarrer les données brutes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3149">Raw Data Start VA</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3150">Adresse de départ du modèle TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3150">The starting address of the TLS template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3151">Le modèle est un bloc de données utilisé pour initialiser les données TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3151">The template is a block of data that is used to initialize TLS data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3152">Le système copie toutes ces données chaque fois qu’un thread est créé, donc il ne doit pas être endommagé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3152">The system copies all of this data each time a thread is created, so it must not be corrupted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3153">Notez que cette adresse n’est pas un RVA. Il s’agit d’une adresse pour laquelle il doit y avoir un réadressage de base dans la section. reloc.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3153">Note that this address is not an RVA; it is an address for which there should be a base relocation in the .reloc section.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3154">4/8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3154">4/8</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3155">4/8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3155">4/8</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3156">Fin des données brutes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3156">Raw Data End VA</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3157">Adresse du dernier octet du TLS, à l’exception du remplissage zéro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3157">The address of the last byte of the TLS, except for the zero fill.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3158">Comme avec le champ de VA de début des données brutes, il s’agit d’un VA, et non d’un RVA.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3158">As with the Raw Data Start VA field, this is a VA, not an RVA.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3159">8/16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3159">8/16</span></span> <br/>     | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3160">4/8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3160">4/8</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3161">Adresse de l’index</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3161">Address of Index</span></span> <br/>     | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3162">Emplacement de réception de l’index TLS que le chargeur affecte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3162">The location to receive the TLS index, which the loader assigns.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3163">Cet emplacement se trouve dans une section de données ordinaire et peut donc recevoir un nom symbolique accessible au programme.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3163">This location is in an ordinary data section, so it can be given a symbolic name that is accessible to the program.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                    |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3164">12/24</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3164">12/24</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3165">4/8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3165">4/8</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3166">Adresse des rappels</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3166">Address of Callbacks</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3167">Pointeur vers un tableau de fonctions de rappel TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3167">The pointer to an array of TLS callback functions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3168">Le tableau se termine par un caractère NULL ; par conséquent, si aucune fonction de rappel n’est prise en charge, ce champ pointe vers la valeur zéro pour 4 octets.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3168">The array is null-terminated, so if no callback function is supported, this field points to 4 bytes set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3169">Pour plus d’informations sur le prototype de ces fonctions, consultez [fonctions de rappel TLS](#tls-callback-functions).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3169">For information about the prototype for these functions, see [TLS Callback Functions](#tls-callback-functions).</span></span><br/>                                                      |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3170">16/32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3170">16/32</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3171">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3171">4</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3172">Taille de remplissage zéro</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3172">Size of Zero Fill</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3173">Taille en octets du modèle, au-delà des données initialisées, délimitées par les champs de début et de fin des données brutes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3173">The size in bytes of the template, beyond the initialized data delimited by the Raw Data Start VA and Raw Data End VA fields.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3174">La taille totale du modèle doit être identique à la taille totale des données TLS dans le fichier image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3174">The total template size should be the same as the total size of TLS data in the image file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3175">Le remplissage zéro correspond à la quantité de données qui vient après les données non null initialisées.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3175">The zero fill is the amount of data that comes after the initialized nonzero data.</span></span> <br/>                            |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3176">20/36</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3176">20/36</span></span> <br/>    | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3177">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3177">4</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3178">Caractéristiques</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3178">Characteristics</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3179">Les quatre bits \[ 23:20 \] décrivent les informations d’alignement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3179">The four bits \[23:20\] describe alignment info.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3180">Les valeurs possibles sont celles définies comme IMAGE \_ SCN \_ align \_ \* , qui sont également utilisées pour décrire l’alignement de la section dans les fichiers objets.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3180">Possible values are those defined as IMAGE\_SCN\_ALIGN\_\*, which are also used to describe alignment of section in object files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3181">Les 28 autres bits sont réservés pour une utilisation ultérieure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3181">The other 28 bits are reserved for future use.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                       |



 

#### <a name="tls-callback-functions"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3182">Fonctions de rappel TLS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3182">TLS Callback Functions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3183">Le programme peut fournir une ou plusieurs fonctions de rappel TLS pour prendre en charge l’initialisation et l’arrêt supplémentaires pour les objets de données TLS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3183">The program can provide one or more TLS callback functions to support additional initialization and termination for TLS data objects.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3184">Une utilisation classique pour une telle fonction de rappel consisterait à appeler des constructeurs et des destructeurs pour les objets.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3184">A typical use for such a callback function would be to call constructors and destructors for objects.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3185">Bien qu’il n’y ait généralement pas plus d’une fonction de rappel, un rappel est implémenté en tant que tableau pour permettre l’ajout de fonctions de rappel supplémentaires si vous le souhaitez.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3185">Although there is typically no more than one callback function, a callback is implemented as an array to make it possible to add additional callback functions if desired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3186">S’il existe plusieurs fonctions de rappel, chaque fonction est appelée dans l’ordre dans lequel son adresse apparaît dans le tableau.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3186">If there is more than one callback function, each function is called in the order in which its address appears in the array.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3187">Un pointeur null termine le tableau.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3187">A null pointer terminates the array.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3188">Il est tout à fait possible d’avoir une liste vide (aucun rappel pris en charge), auquel cas le tableau de rappel a un seul membre, un pointeur null.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3188">It is perfectly valid to have an empty list (no callback supported), in which case the callback array has exactly one member-a null pointer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3189">Le prototype d’une fonction de rappel (pointée par un pointeur de type PIMAGE \_ TLS \_ callback) a les mêmes paramètres qu’une fonction de point d’entrée dll :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3189">The prototype for a callback function (pointed to by a pointer of type PIMAGE\_TLS\_CALLBACK) has the same parameters as a DLL entry-point function:</span></span>


```C++
typedef VOID
(NTAPI *PIMAGE_TLS_CALLBACK) (
    PVOID DllHandle,
    DWORD Reason,
    PVOID Reserved
    );
```



<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3190">Le paramètre réservé doit être défini à zéro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3190">The Reserved parameter should be set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3191">Le paramètre Reason peut prendre les valeurs suivantes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3191">The Reason parameter can take the following values:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3192">Paramètre</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3192">Setting</span></span>                          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3193">Valeur</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3193">Value</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3194">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3194">Description</span></span>                                                                                          |
|----------------------------------|---------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3195">\_attachement du processus dll \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3195">DLL\_PROCESS\_ATTACH</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3196">1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3196">1</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3197">Un nouveau processus a démarré, y compris le premier thread.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3197">A new process has started, including the first thread.</span></span> <br/>                                   |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3198">\_attachement de thread dll \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3198">DLL\_THREAD\_ATTACH</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3199">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3199">2</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3200">Un nouveau thread a été créé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3200">A new thread has been created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3201">Cette notification est envoyée pour tous les threads à l’exception du premier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3201">This notification sent for all but the first thread.</span></span> <br/>      |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3202">\_détachement de thread dll \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3202">DLL\_THREAD\_DETACH</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3203">3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3203">3</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3204">Un thread va être arrêté.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3204">A thread is about to be terminated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3205">Cette notification est envoyée pour tous les threads à l’exception du premier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3205">This notification sent for all but the first thread.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3206">\_détachement de processus dll \_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3206">DLL\_PROCESS\_DETACH</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3207">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3207">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3208">Un processus va se terminer, y compris le thread d’origine.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3208">A process is about to terminate, including the original thread.</span></span> <br/>                          |



 

### <a name="the-load-configuration-structure-image-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3209">Structure de la configuration de charge (image uniquement)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3209">The Load Configuration Structure (Image Only)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3210">La structure de la configuration de chargement (répertoire de configuration de \_ chargement \_ d’image \_ ) était précédemment utilisée dans des cas très limités dans le système d’exploitation Windows NT lui-même pour décrire les différentes fonctionnalités trop difficiles ou trop grandes pour être décrites dans l’en-tête de fichier ou l’en-tête facultatif de l’image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3210">The load configuration structure (IMAGE\_LOAD\_CONFIG\_DIRECTORY) was formerly used in very limited cases in the Windows NT operating system itself to describe various features too difficult or too large to describe in the file header or optional header of the image.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3211">Les versions actuelles de Microsoft Linker et Windows XP et les versions ultérieures de Windows utilisent une nouvelle version de cette structure pour les systèmes x86 32 bits qui incluent la technologie SEH réservée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3211">Current versions of the Microsoft linker and Windows XP and later versions of Windows use a new version of this structure for 32-bit x86-based systems that include reserved SEH technology.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3212">Fournit la liste des gestionnaires d’exceptions structurés sécurisés que le système d’exploitation utilise pendant la distribution des exceptions.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3212">This provides a list of safe structured exception handlers that the operating system uses during exception dispatching.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3213">Si l’adresse du gestionnaire réside dans la plage de VA d’une image et si elle est marquée comme étant réservée à la gestion de la gestion des exceptions (autrement dit, l’IMAGE \_ DLLCHARACTERISTICS \_ non \_ SEH n’est pas claire dans le champ DLLCHARACTERISTICS de l’en-tête facultatif, comme décrit précédemment), le gestionnaire doit figurer dans la liste des gestionnaires sécurisés connus pour cette image.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3213">If the handler address resides in an image's VA range and is marked as reserved SEH-aware (that is, IMAGE\_DLLCHARACTERISTICS\_NO\_SEH is clear in the DllCharacteristics field of the optional header, as described earlier), then the handler must be in the list of known safe handlers for that image.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3214">Dans le cas contraire, le système d’exploitation met fin à l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3214">Otherwise, the operating system terminates the application.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3215">Cela permet d’éviter l’exploit « détournement du gestionnaire d’exceptions x86 » qui a été utilisé par le passé pour prendre le contrôle du système d’exploitation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3215">This helps prevent the "x86 exception handler hijacking" exploit that has been used in the past to take control of the operating system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3216">L’éditeur de liens de Microsoft fournit automatiquement une structure de configuration de charge par défaut pour inclure les données SEH réservées.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3216">The Microsoft linker automatically provides a default load configuration structure to include the reserved SEH data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3217">Si le code utilisateur fournit déjà une structure de configuration de charge, il doit inclure les nouveaux champs SEH réservés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3217">If the user code already provides a load configuration structure, it must include the new reserved SEH fields.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3218">Dans le cas contraire, l’éditeur de liens ne peut pas inclure les données SEH réservées et l’image n’est pas marquée comme contenant la fonction SEH réservée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3218">Otherwise, the linker cannot include the reserved SEH data and the image is not marked as containing reserved SEH.</span></span>

#### <a name="load-configuration-directory"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3219">Charger le répertoire de configuration</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3219">Load Configuration Directory</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3220">L’entrée de répertoire de données pour une structure de configuration de chargement SEH préréservée doit spécifier une taille particulière de la structure de la configuration de charge, car le chargeur du système d’exploitation s’attend toujours à une certaine valeur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3220">The data directory entry for a pre-reserved SEH load configuration structure must specify a particular size of the load configuration structure because the operating system loader always expects it to be a certain value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3221">À cet égard, la taille est véritablement uniquement une vérification de version.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3221">In that regard, the size is really only a version check.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3222">Pour la compatibilité avec Windows XP et les versions antérieures de Windows, la taille doit être de 64 pour les images x86.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3222">For compatibility with Windows XP and earlier versions of Windows, the size must be 64 for x86 images.</span></span>

#### <a name="load-configuration-layout"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3223">Charger la disposition de configuration</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3223">Load Configuration Layout</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3224">La structure de la configuration de chargement présente la disposition suivante pour les fichiers PE 32 bits et 64 bits :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3224">The load configuration structure has the following layout for 32-bit and 64-bit PE files:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3225">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3225">Offset</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3226">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3226">Size</span></span>            | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3227">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3227">Field</span></span>                                      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3228">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3228">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
|---------------------|-----------------|--------------------------------------------|---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3229">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3229">0</span></span> <br/>       | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3230">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3230">4</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3231">Caractéristiques</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3231">Characteristics</span></span> <br/>                | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3232">Indicateurs qui indiquent les attributs du fichier, actuellement inutilisés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3232">Flags that indicate attributes of the file, currently unused.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                   |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3233">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3233">4</span></span> <br/>       | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3234">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3234">4</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3235">TimeDateStamp</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3235">TimeDateStamp</span></span> <br/>                  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3236">Valeur d’horodatage de date et d’heure.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3236">Date and time stamp value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3237">La valeur est représentée dans le nombre de secondes qui se sont écoulées depuis minuit (00:00:00), le 1er janvier 1970, heure UTC (Universal Coordinated Time), en fonction de l’horloge système.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3237">The value is represented in the number of seconds that have elapsed since midnight (00:00:00), January 1, 1970, Universal Coordinated Time, according to the system clock.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3238">L’horodatage peut être imprimé à l’aide de la fonction Time du runtime C (CRT).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3238">The time stamp can be printed by using the C runtime (CRT) time function.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3239">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3239">8</span></span> <br/>       | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3240">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3240">2</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3241">MajorVersion</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3241">MajorVersion</span></span> <br/>                   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3242">Numéro de version principale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3242">Major version number.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3243">10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3243">10</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3244">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3244">2</span></span> <br/>   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3245">MinorVersion</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3245">MinorVersion</span></span> <br/>                   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3246">Numéro de version secondaire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3246">Minor version number.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
