<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3352">Le champ GuardFlags contient une combinaison d’un ou plusieurs des indicateurs et sous-champs suivants :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3352">The GuardFlags field contains a combination of one or more of the following flags and subfields:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3353">Module effectue des vérifications de l’intégrité du workflow à l’aide de la prise en charge fournie par le système.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3353">Module performs control flow integrity checks using system-supplied support.</span></span>

    ` #define IMAGE_GUARD_CF_INSTRUMENTED  0x00000100`

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3354">Le module effectue des contrôles de workflow et d’intégrité en écriture.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3354">Module performs control flow and write integrity checks.</span></span>

    ` #define IMAGE_GUARD_CFW_INSTRUMENTED  0x00000200`

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3355">Le module contient des métadonnées cibles de workflow de contrôle valides.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3355">Module contains valid control flow target metadata.</span></span>

    `#define IMAGE_GUARD_CF_FUNCTION_TABLE_PRESENT  0x00000400`

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3356">Le module n’utilise pas le cookie de sécurité/GS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3356">Module does not make use of the /GS security cookie.</span></span>

    ` #define IMAGE_GUARD_SECURITY_COOKIE_UNUSED  0x00000800`

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3357">Le module prend en charge l’IAT de chargement différé en lecture seule.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3357">Module supports read only delay load IAT.</span></span>

    `#define IMAGE_GUARD_PROTECT_DELAYLOAD_IAT  0x00001000`

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3358">DELAYLOAD Import table dans sa propre section. didat (avec rien d’autre) qui peut être reprotégé librement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3358">Delayload import table in its own .didat section (with nothing else in it) that can be freely reprotected.</span></span>

    ` #define IMAGE_GUARD_DELAYLOAD_IAT_IN_ITS_OWN_SECTION  0x00002000`

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3359">Le module contient des informations d’exportation supprimées.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3359">Module contains suppressed export information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3360">Cela déduit également que la table IAT Address comprise est également présente dans la configuration de chargement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3360">This also infers that the address taken IAT table is also present in the load config.</span></span>

    `#define  IMAGE_GUARD_CF_EXPORT_SUPPRESSION_INFO_PRESENT  0x00004000`

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3361">Le module permet la suppression des exportations.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3361">Module enables suppression of exports.</span></span>

    `#define IMAGE_GUARD_CF_ENABLE_EXPORT_SUPPRESSION  0x00008000`

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3362">Le module contient des informations sur la cible longjmp.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3362">Module contains longjmp target information.</span></span>

    ` #define IMAGE_GUARD_CF_LONGJUMP_TABLE_PRESENT  0x00010000`

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3363">Masque pour le sous-champ qui contient le Stride des entrées de la table de fonctions de protection du workflow de contrôle (autrement dit, le nombre supplémentaire d’octets par entrée de table).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3363">Mask for the subfield that contains the stride of Control Flow Guard function table entries (that is, the additional count of bytes per table entry).</span></span>

    ` #define IMAGE_GUARD_CF_FUNCTION_TABLE_SIZE_MASK  0xF0000000`

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3364">En outre, l’SDK Windows en-tête Winnt. h définit cette macro pour le nombre de bits de décalage vers la droite de la valeur GuardFlags pour la justification à droite du tableau de la fonction de protection du workflow de contrôle Stride :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3364">Additionally, the Windows SDK winnt.h header defines this macro for the amount of bits to right-shift the GuardFlags value to right-justify the Control Flow Guard function table stride:</span></span>

` #define IMAGE_GUARD_CF_FUNCTION_TABLE_SIZE_SHIFT  28`

### <a name="the-rsrc-section"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3365">Section. rsrc</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3365">The .rsrc Section</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3366">Les ressources sont indexées par une structure d’arborescence triée binaire à plusieurs niveaux.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3366">Resources are indexed by a multiple-level binary-sorted tree structure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3367">La conception générale peut incorporer 2 \* \* 31 niveaux.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3367">The general design can incorporate 2\*\*31 levels.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3368">Par Convention, toutefois, Windows utilise trois niveaux :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3368">By convention, however, Windows uses three levels:</span></span>

<dl> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3369">Type</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3369">Type</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3370">Nom</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3370">Name</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3371">Language</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3371">Language</span></span>  
</dl>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3372">Une série de tables de répertoires de ressources relient tous les niveaux de la manière suivante : chaque table de répertoires est suivie d’une série d’entrées de répertoire qui fournissent le nom ou l’identificateur (ID) de ce niveau (type, nom ou niveau de langage) et une adresse de description de données ou une autre table de répertoire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3372">A series of resource directory tables relates all of the levels in the following way: Each directory table is followed by a series of directory entries that give the name or identifier (ID) for that level (Type, Name, or Language level) and an address of either a data description or another directory table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3373">Si l’adresse pointe vers une description de données, les données sont une feuille dans l’arborescence.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3373">If the address points to a data description, then the data is a leaf in the tree.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3374">Si l’adresse pointe vers une autre table de répertoire, cette table répertorie les entrées de répertoire au niveau supérieur suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3374">If the address points to another directory table, then that table lists directory entries at the next level down.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3375">Les ID de type, de nom et de langue d’une feuille sont déterminés par le chemin d’accès utilisé par les tables de répertoires pour atteindre la feuille.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3375">A leaf's Type, Name, and Language IDs are determined by the path that is taken through directory tables to reach the leaf.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3376">La première table détermine l’ID de type, la deuxième table (désignée par l’entrée de répertoire de la première table), et la troisième table détermine l’ID de langue.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3376">The first table determines Type ID, the second table (pointed to by the directory entry in the first table) determines Name ID, and the third table determines Language ID.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3377">La structure générale de la section. rsrc est la suivante :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3377">The general structure of the .rsrc section is:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3378">Données</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3378">Data</span></span>                                                                   | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3379">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3379">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                           |
|------------------------------------------------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3380">Tables de répertoires de ressources (et entrées de répertoire de ressources)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3380">Resource Directory Tables (and Resource Directory Entries)</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3381">Une série de tables, une pour chaque groupe de nœuds dans l’arborescence.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3381">A series of tables, one for each group of nodes in the tree.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3382">Tous les nœuds de niveau supérieur (type) sont répertoriés dans le premier tableau.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3382">All top-level (Type) nodes are listed in the first table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3383">Les entrées de ce tableau pointent vers les tables de second niveau.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3383">Entries in this table point to second-level tables.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3384">Chaque arborescence de second niveau a le même ID de type mais des ID de noms différents.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3384">Each second-level tree has the same Type ID but different Name IDs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3385">Les arborescences de troisième niveau ont les mêmes ID de type et de nom, mais des ID de langue différents.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3385">Third-level trees have the same Type and Name IDs but different Language IDs.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3386">Chaque table individuelle est immédiatement suivie d’entrées de répertoire, dans lesquelles chaque entrée a un nom ou un identificateur numérique et un pointeur vers une description de données ou une table au niveau inférieur suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3386">Each individual table is immediately followed by directory entries, in which each entry has a name or numeric identifier and a pointer to a data description or a table at the next lower level.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3387">Chaînes de répertoire de ressources</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3387">Resource Directory Strings</span></span> <br/>                                 | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3388">Chaînes Unicode alignées sur deux octets, qui servent de données de chaîne pointées par des entrées de répertoire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3388">Two-byte-aligned Unicode strings, which serve as string data that is pointed to by directory entries.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3389">Description des données de ressource</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3389">Resource Data Description</span></span> <br/>                                  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3390">Tableau d’enregistrements, désigné par des tables, qui décrivent la taille et l’emplacement réels des données de ressource.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3390">An array of records, pointed to by tables, that describe the actual size and location of the resource data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3391">Ces enregistrements sont les feuilles de l’arborescence de la description des ressources.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3391">These records are the leaves in the resource-description tree.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3392">Données de ressource</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3392">Resource Data</span></span> <br/>                                              | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3393">Données brutes de la section de la ressource.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3393">Raw data of the resource section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3394">Les informations relatives à la taille et à l’emplacement dans le champ descriptions des données de ressource délimitent les régions individuelles des données de ressource.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3394">The size and location information in the Resource Data Descriptions field delimit the individual regions of resource data.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |



 

#### <a name="resource-directory-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3395">Table de répertoire des ressources</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3395">Resource Directory Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3396">Chaque table de répertoire de ressources a le format suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3396">Each resource directory table has the following format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3397">Cette structure de données doit être considérée comme l’en-tête d’une table, car la table se compose en fait d’entrées de répertoire (décrites dans la section 6.9.2, « entrées de répertoire de ressources ») et de cette structure :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3397">This data structure should be considered the heading of a table because the table actually consists of directory entries (described in section 6.9.2, "Resource Directory Entries") and this structure:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3398">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3398">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3399">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3399">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3400">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3400">Field</span></span>                              | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3401">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3401">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                     |

#### <a name="resource-directory-entries"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3428">Entrées de répertoire de ressources</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3428">Resource Directory Entries</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3429">Les entrées d’annuaire composent les lignes d’une table.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3429">The directory entries make up the rows of a table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3430">Chaque entrée de répertoire de ressources a le format suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3430">Each resource directory entry has the following format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3431">Le fait que l’entrée soit un nom ou une entrée d’ID est indiqué par la table de répertoire de ressources, qui indique le nombre d’entrées de nom et d’ID suivies (souvenez-vous que toutes les entrées de nom précèdent toutes les entrées d’ID de la table).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3431">Whether the entry is a Name or ID entry is indicated by the resource directory table, which indicates how many Name and ID entries follow it (remember that all the Name entries precede all the ID entries for the table).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3432">Toutes les entrées de la table sont triées dans l’ordre croissant : les entrées de nom par chaîne respectant la casse et les entrées d’ID par valeur numérique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3432">All entries for the table are sorted in ascending order: the Name entries by case-sensitive string and the ID entries by numeric value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3433">Les décalages sont relatifs à l’adresse dans la \_ ressource d’entrée de répertoire d’images \_ \_ DataDirectory.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3433">Offsets are relative to the address in the IMAGE\_DIRECTORY\_ENTRY\_RESOURCE DataDirectory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3434">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [homologation dans le PE : visite guidée du format de fichier exécutable portable Win32](/previous-versions/ms809762(v=msdn.10)#pe-file-resources) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3434">See [Peering Inside the PE: A Tour of the Win32 Portable Executable File Format](/previous-versions/ms809762(v=msdn.10)#pe-file-resources) for more information.</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3435">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3435">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3436">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3436">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3437">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3437">Field</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3438">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3438">Description</span></span>                                                                                                          |
|---------------|---------------|---------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3439">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3439">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3440">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3440">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3441">Décalage du nom</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3441">Name Offset</span></span> <br/>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3442">Offset d’une chaîne qui donne le type, le nom ou l’entrée d’ID de langue, en fonction du niveau de la table.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3442">The offset of a string that gives the Type, Name, or Language ID entry, depending on level of table.</span></span> <br/>     |

| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3452">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3452">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3453">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3453">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3454">Décalage de sous-répertoire</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3454">Subdirectory Offset</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3455">Bit 1 élevé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3455">High bit 1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3456">Les 31 bits inférieurs sont l’adresse d’une autre table de répertoire de ressources (le niveau inférieur suivant).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3456">The lower 31 bits are the address of another resource directory table (the next level down).</span></span> <br/> |



 

#### <a name="resource-directory-string"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3457">Chaîne du répertoire de ressources</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3457">Resource Directory String</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3458">La zone de la chaîne du répertoire de ressources se compose de chaînes Unicode, alignées sur les mots.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3458">The resource directory string area consists of Unicode strings, which are word-aligned.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3459">Ces chaînes sont stockées ensemble après la dernière entrée de répertoire de ressources et avant la première entrée de données de ressource.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3459">These strings are stored together after the last Resource Directory entry and before the first Resource Data entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3460">Cela réduit l’impact de ces chaînes de longueur variable sur l’alignement des entrées de répertoire de taille fixe.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3460">This minimizes the impact of these variable-length strings on the alignment of the fixed-size directory entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3461">Chaque chaîne de répertoire de ressources a le format suivant :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3461">Each resource directory string has the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3462">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3462">Offset</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3463">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3463">Size</span></span>                 | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3464">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3464">Field</span></span>                      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3465">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3465">Description</span></span>                                                            |
|---------------|----------------------|----------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3466">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3466">0</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3467">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3467">2</span></span> <br/>        | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3468">Longueur</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3468">Length</span></span> <br/>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3469">Taille de la chaîne, sans inclure le champ de longueur lui-même.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3469">The size of the string, not including length field itself.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3470">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3470">2</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3471">variable</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3471">variable</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3472">Chaîne Unicode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3472">Unicode String</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3473">Données de chaîne Unicode de longueur variable, alignées sur les mots.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3473">The variable-length Unicode string data, word-aligned.</span></span> <br/>     |



 

#### <a name="resource-data-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3474">Entrée de données de ressource</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3474">Resource Data Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3475">Chaque entrée de données de ressource décrit une unité réelle de données brutes dans la zone de données de ressource.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3475">Each Resource Data entry describes an actual unit of raw data in the Resource Data area.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3476">Une entrée de données de ressource a le format suivant :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3476">A Resource Data entry has the following format:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3477">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3477">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3478">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3478">Size</span></span>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3479">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3479">Field</span></span>                            | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3480">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3480">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                           |
|----------------|---------------|----------------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3481">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3481">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3482">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3482">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3483">RVA de données</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3483">Data RVA</span></span> <br/>             | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3484">Adresse d’une unité de données de ressource dans la zone de données de ressource.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3484">The address of a unit of resource data in the Resource Data area.</span></span> <br/>                                                                         |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3485">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3485">4</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3486">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3486">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3487">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3487">Size</span></span> <br/>                 | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3488">Taille, en octets, des données de ressource vers lesquelles pointe le champ de RVA de données.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3488">The size, in bytes, of the resource data that is pointed to by the Data RVA field.</span></span> <br/>                                                        |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3489">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3489">8</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3490">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3490">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3491">codepage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3491">Codepage</span></span> <br/>             | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3492">Page de codes utilisée pour décoder les valeurs de point de code dans les données de ressource.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3492">The code page that is used to decode code point values within the resource data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3493">En règle générale, la page de codes est la page de codes Unicode.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3493">Typically, the code page would be the Unicode code page.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3494">12</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3494">12</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3495">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3495">4</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3496">Réservé, doit avoir la valeur 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3496">Reserved, must be 0.</span></span> <br/> |                                                                                                                                                       |



 

### <a name="the-cormeta-section-object-only"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3497">Section. cormeta (objet uniquement)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3497">The .cormeta Section (Object Only)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3498">Les métadonnées CLR sont stockées dans cette section.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3498">CLR metadata is stored in this section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3499">Il est utilisé pour indiquer que le fichier objet contient du code managé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3499">It is used to indicate that the object file contains managed code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3500">Le format des métadonnées n’est pas documenté, mais peut être transmis aux interfaces CLR pour la gestion des métadonnées.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3500">The format of the metadata is not documented, but can be handed to the CLR interfaces for handling metadata.</span></span>

### <a name="the-sxdata-section"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3501">Section. sxdata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3501">The .sxdata Section</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3502">Les gestionnaires d’exceptions valides d’un objet sont répertoriés dans la section **. sxdata** de cet objet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3502">The valid exception handlers of an object are listed in the **.sxdata** section of that object.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3503">La section est marquée comme IMAGE \_ SCN \_ LNK \_ info.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3503">The section is marked IMAGE\_SCN\_LNK\_INFO.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3504">Il contient l’index de symboles COFF de chaque gestionnaire valide, en utilisant 4 octets par index.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3504">It contains the COFF symbol index of each valid handler, using 4 bytes per index.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3505">En outre, le compilateur marque un objet COFF comme étant inscrit SEH en émettant le symbole absolu « @feat.00 » avec le LSB du champ de valeur défini sur 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3505">Additionally, the compiler marks a COFF object as registered SEH by emitting the absolute symbol "@feat.00" with the LSB of the value field set to 1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3506">Un objet COFF sans gestionnaires SEH inscrits aurait le @feat.00 symbole «», mais pas la section **. sxdata** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3506">A COFF object with no registered SEH handlers would have the "@feat.00" symbol, but no **.sxdata** section.</span></span>

## <a name="archive-library-file-format"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3507">Format de fichier d’archive (bibliothèque)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3507">Archive (Library) File Format</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3508">Signature du fichier d’archive</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3508">Archive File Signature</span></span>](#archive-file-signature)
- [<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3509">Archiver les en-têtes de membres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3509">Archive Member Headers</span></span>](#archive-member-headers)
- [<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3510">Premier membre de l’éditeur de liens</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3510">First Linker Member</span></span>](#first-linker-member)
- [<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3511">Deuxième membre de l’éditeur de liens</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3511">Second Linker Member</span></span>](#second-linker-member)
- [<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3512">Membre Longnames</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3512">Longnames Member</span></span>](#longnames-member)

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3513">Le format d’archive COFF fournit un mécanisme standard pour le stockage des collections de fichiers objets.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3513">The COFF archive format provides a standard mechanism for storing collections of object files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3514">Ces collections sont communément appelées bibliothèques dans la documentation de programmation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3514">These collections are commonly called libraries in programming documentation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3515">Les 8 premiers octets d’une archive sont composés de la signature de fichier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3515">The first 8 bytes of an archive consist of the file signature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3516">Le reste de l’archive est constitué d’une série de membres d’archive, comme suit :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3516">The rest of the archive consists of a series of archive members, as follows:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3517">Les premier et deuxième membres sont « membres de l’éditeur de liens ».</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3517">The first and second members are "linker members."</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3518">Chacun de ces membres a son propre format comme décrit dans la section [type de nom d’importation](#import-name-type).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3518">Each of these members has its own format as described in section [Import Name Type](#import-name-type).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3519">En règle générale, un éditeur de liens place des informations dans ces membres d’archive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3519">Typically, a linker places information into these archive members.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3520">Les membres de l’éditeur de liens contiennent le répertoire de l’archive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3520">The linker members contain the directory of the archive.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3521">Le troisième membre est le membre « longnames ».</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3521">The third member is the "longnames" member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3522">Ce membre facultatif se compose d’une série de chaînes ASCII se terminant par un caractère null, dans lesquelles chaque chaîne est le nom d’un autre membre d’archive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3522">This optional member consists of a series of null-terminated ASCII strings in which each string is the name of another archive member.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3523">Le reste de l’archive est constitué de membres standard (fichier objet).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3523">The rest of the archive consists of standard (object-file) members.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3524">Chacun de ces membres contient le contenu d’un fichier objet dans son intégralité.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3524">Each of these members contains the contents of one object file in its entirety.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3525">Un en-tête de membre d’archive précède chaque membre.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3525">An archive member header precedes each member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3526">La liste suivante présente la structure générale d’une archive :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3526">The following list shows the general structure of an archive:</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3527">Signature : « ! &lt; arch &gt; \\ n»</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3527">Signature :"!&lt;arch&gt;\\n"</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3528">En-tête</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3528">Header</span></span>

    <dl> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3529">premier membre de l’éditeur de liens</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3529">1st Linker Member</span></span>  
    </dl>

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3530">En-tête</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3530">Header</span></span>

    <dl> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3531">2e membre de l’éditeur de liens</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3531">2nd Linker Member</span></span>  
    </dl>

-   <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3532">En-tête</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3532">Header</span></span>

### <a name="archive-file-signature"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3540">Signature du fichier d’archive</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3540">Archive File Signature</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3541">La signature du fichier d’archive identifie le type de fichier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3541">The archive file signature identifies the file type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3542">Tout utilitaire (par exemple, un éditeur de liens) qui prend un fichier d’archive comme entrée peut vérifier le type de fichier en lisant cette signature.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3542">Any utility (for example, a linker) that takes an archive file as input can check the file type by reading this signature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3543">La signature se compose des caractères ASCII suivants, dans lesquels chaque caractère ci-dessous est représenté littéralement, à l’exception du caractère de saut de ligne ( \\ n) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3543">The signature consists of the following ASCII characters, in which each character below is represented literally, except for the newline (\\n) character:</span></span>

`!<arch>\n`

### <a name="archive-member-headers"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3544">Archiver les en-têtes de membres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3544">Archive Member Headers</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3545">Chaque membre (éditeur de liens, longnames ou membre de fichier objet) est précédé d’un en-tête.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3545">Each member (linker, longnames, or object-file member) is preceded by a header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3546">Un en-tête de membre d’archive a le format suivant, où chaque champ est une chaîne de texte ASCII qui est justifiée à gauche et complétée par des espaces à la fin du champ.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3546">An archive member header has the following format, in which each field is an ASCII text string that is left justified and padded with spaces to the end of the field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3547">Il n’y a pas de caractère null de fin dans l’un de ces champs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3547">There is no terminating null character in any of these fields.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3548">Chaque en-tête de membre commence sur la première adresse paire après la fin du membre Archive précédent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3548">Each member header starts on the first even address after the end of the previous archive member.</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3549">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3549">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3550">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3550">Size</span></span>           | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3551">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3551">Field</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3552">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3552">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                 |
|----------------|----------------|---------------------------|-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3553">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3553">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3554">16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3554">16</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3555">Nom</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3555">Name</span></span> <br/>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3556">Nom du membre d’archive, avec une barre oblique (/) ajoutée pour terminer le nom.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3556">The name of the archive member, with a slash (/) appended to terminate the name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3557">Si le premier caractère est une barre oblique, le nom a une interprétation spéciale, comme décrit dans le tableau suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3557">If the first character is a slash, the name has a special interpretation, as described in the following table.</span></span> <br/> |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3558">16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3558">16</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3559">12</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3559">12</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3560">Date</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3560">Date</span></span> <br/>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3561">Date et heure de création du membre d’archive : il s’agit de la représentation décimale ASCII du nombre de secondes écoulées depuis le 1/1/1970 UCT.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3561">The date and time that the archive member was created: This is the ASCII decimal representation of the number of seconds since 1/1/1970 UCT.</span></span> <br/>                                                    |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3562">28</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3562">28</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3563">6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3563">6</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3564">ID d'utilisateur</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3564">User ID</span></span> <br/>       | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3565">Représentation décimale ASCII de l’ID d’utilisateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3565">An ASCII decimal representation of the user ID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3566">Ce champ ne contient pas de valeur significative sur les plateformes Windows, car les outils Microsoft émettent tous les espaces.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3566">This field does not contain a meaningful value on Windows platforms because Microsoft tools emit all blanks.</span></span> <br/>                                    |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3567">34</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3567">34</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3568">6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3568">6</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3569">ID de groupe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3569">Group ID</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3570">Représentation décimale ASCII de l’ID de groupe.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3570">An ASCII decimal representation of the group ID.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3571">Ce champ ne contient pas de valeur significative sur les plateformes Windows, car les outils Microsoft émettent tous les espaces.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3571">This field does not contain a meaningful value on Windows platforms because Microsoft tools emit all blanks.</span></span> <br/>                                   |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3572">40</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3572">40</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3573">8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3573">8</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3574">Mode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3574">Mode</span></span> <br/>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3575">Représentation octale ASCII du mode de fichier du membre.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3575">An ASCII octal representation of the member's file mode.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3576">Il s’agit \_ de la valeur du mode St de la fonction Runtime C \_ wstat.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3576">This is the ST\_MODE value from the C run-time function \_wstat.</span></span> <br/>                                                                       |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3577">48</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3577">48</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3578">10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3578">10</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3579">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3579">Size</span></span> <br/>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3580">Représentation décimale ASCII de la taille totale du membre d’archive, à l’exclusion de la taille de l’en-tête.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3580">An ASCII decimal representation of the total size of the archive member, not including the size of the header.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                  |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3581">58</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3581">58</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3582">2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3582">2</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3583">Fin d’en-tête</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3583">End of Header</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3584">Les deux octets de la chaîne C « ̃ \\ n » (0X60 0x0A).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3584">The two bytes in the C string "˜\\n" (0x60 0x0A).</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                               |



 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3585">Le champ nom a l’un des formats répertoriés dans le tableau suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3585">The Name field has one of the formats shown in the following table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3586">Comme mentionné précédemment, chacune de ces chaînes est alignée à gauche et complétée par des espaces de fin dans un champ de 16 octets :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3586">As mentioned earlier, each of these strings is left justified and padded with trailing spaces within a field of 16 bytes:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3587">Contenu du champ de nom</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3587">Contents of Name field</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3588">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3588">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
|------------------------|------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3589">nomme</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3589">name/</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3590">Nom du membre d’archive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3590">The name of the archive member.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| / <br/>          | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3591">Le membre archive est l’un des deux membres de l’éditeur de liens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3591">The archive member is one of the two linker members.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3592">Les deux membres de l’éditeur de liens portent ce nom.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3592">Both of the linker members have this name.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                          |
| // <br/>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3593">Le membre archive est le membre longnames, qui se compose d’une série de chaînes ASCII se terminant par null.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3593">The archive member is the longnames member, which consists of a series of null-terminated ASCII strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3594">Le membre longnames est le troisième membre Archive et est facultatif.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3594">The longnames member is the third archive member and is optional.</span></span> <br/>                                                                     |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3595">/n</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3595">/n</span></span> <br/>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3596">Le nom du membre d’archive se trouve au décalage n dans le membre longnames.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3596">The name of the archive member is located at offset n within the longnames member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3597">Le nombre n est la représentation décimale du décalage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3597">The number n is the decimal representation of the offset.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3598">Par exemple : « /26 » indique que le nom du membre d’archive se trouve à 26 octets au-delà du début du contenu du membre longnames.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3598">For example: "/26" indicates that the name of the archive member is located 26 bytes beyond the beginning of the longnames member contents.</span></span> <br/> |



 

### <a name="first-linker-member"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3599">Premier membre de l’éditeur de liens</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3599">First Linker Member</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3600">Le nom du premier membre de l’éditeur de liens est « / ».</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3600">The name of the first linker member is "/".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3601">Le premier membre de l’éditeur de liens est inclus à des fins de compatibilité descendante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3601">The first linker member is included for backward compatibility.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3602">Elle n’est pas utilisée par les éditeur de liens actuels, mais son format doit être correct.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3602">It is not used by current linkers, but its format must be correct.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3603">Ce membre de l’éditeur de liens fournit un répertoire de noms de symboles, comme le deuxième membre de l’éditeur de liens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3603">This linker member provides a directory of symbol names, as does the second linker member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3604">Pour chaque symbole, les informations indiquent où trouver le membre d’archive contenant le symbole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3604">For each symbol, the information indicates where to find the archive member that contains the symbol.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3605">Le premier membre de l’éditeur de liens a le format suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3605">The first linker member has the following format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3606">Ces informations apparaissent après l’en-tête :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3606">This information appears after the header:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3607">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3607">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3608">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3608">Size</span></span>               | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3609">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3609">Field</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3610">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3610">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
|----------------|--------------------|-------------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3611">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3611">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3612">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3612">4</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3613">Nombre de symboles</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3613">Number of Symbols</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3614">Unsigned long qui contient le nombre de symboles indexés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3614">Unsigned long that contains the number of indexed symbols.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3615">Ce nombre est stocké au format Big-endian.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3615">This number is stored in big-endian format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3616">Chaque membre de fichier d’objet définit généralement un ou plusieurs symboles externes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3616">Each object-file member typically defines one or more external symbols.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                         |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3617">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3617">4</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3618">4 \* n</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3618">4 \* n</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3619">Décalages</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3619">Offsets</span></span> <br/>           | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3620">Tableau d’offsets de fichier pour archiver les en-têtes de membre, où n est égal au nombre de symboles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3620">An array of file offsets to archive member headers, in which n is equal to the Number of Symbols field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3621">Chaque nombre dans le tableau est un entier long non signé, stocké au format Big-endian.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3621">Each number in the array is an unsigned long stored in big-endian format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3622">Pour chaque symbole nommé dans la table de chaînes, l’élément correspondant dans le tableau offsets donne l’emplacement du membre d’archive qui contient le symbole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3622">For each symbol that is named in the string table, the corresponding element in the offsets array gives the location of the archive member that contains the symbol.</span></span> <br/> |
| \* <br/> | \* <br/>     | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3623">Table de chaînes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3623">String Table</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3624">Une série de chaînes terminées par le caractère null qui dénomment tous les symboles dans le répertoire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3624">A series of null-terminated strings that name all the symbols in the directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3625">Chaque chaîne commence immédiatement après le caractère NULL dans la chaîne précédente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3625">Each string begins immediately after the null character in the previous string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3626">Le nombre de chaînes doit être égal à la valeur du champ nombre de symboles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3626">The number of strings must be equal to the value of the Number of Symbols field.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                       |



 

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3627">Les éléments du tableau offsets doivent être disposés par ordre croissant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3627">The elements in the offsets array must be arranged in ascending order.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3628">Cela implique que les symboles de la table de chaînes doivent être organisés en fonction de l’ordre des membres d’archive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3628">This fact implies that the symbols in the string table must be arranged according to the order of archive members.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3629">Par exemple, tous les symboles du premier membre de fichier objet doivent être listés avant les symboles dans le deuxième fichier objet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3629">For example, all the symbols in the first object-file member would have to be listed before the symbols in the second object file.</span></span>

### <a name="second-linker-member"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3630">Deuxième membre de l’éditeur de liens</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3630">Second Linker Member</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3631">Le deuxième membre de l’éditeur de liens a le nom « / » comme le premier membre de l’éditeur de liens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3631">The second linker member has the name "/" as does the first linker member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3632">Bien que les deux membres de l’éditeur de liens fournissent un répertoire des symboles et des membres d’archive qui les contiennent, le deuxième membre de l’éditeur de liens est utilisé de préférence au premier par tous les liens de l’éditeur de liens actuels.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3632">Although both linker members provide a directory of symbols and archive members that contain them, the second linker member is used in preference to the first by all current linkers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3633">Le deuxième membre de l’éditeur de liens comprend des noms de symboles dans l’ordre lexical, ce qui permet une recherche plus rapide par nom.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3633">The second linker member includes symbol names in lexical order, which enables faster searching by name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3634">Le deuxième membre a le format suivant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3634">The second member has the following format.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3635">Ces informations apparaissent après l’en-tête :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3635">This information appears after the header:</span></span>



| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3636">Offset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3636">Offset</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3637">Taille</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3637">Size</span></span>               | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3638">Champ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3638">Field</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3639">Description</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3639">Description</span></span>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
|----------------|--------------------|-------------------------------|----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3640">0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3640">0</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3641">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3641">4</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3642">Nombre de membres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3642">Number of Members</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3643">Valeur non signée de type long qui contient le nombre de membres d’archive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3643">An unsigned long that contains the number of archive members.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                |
| <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3644">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3644">4</span></span> <br/>  | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3645">4 \* m</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3645">4 \* m</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3646">Décalages</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3646">Offsets</span></span> <br/>           | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3647">Tableau d’offsets de fichier pour archiver les en-têtes de membre, organisés dans l’ordre croissant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3647">An array of file offsets to archive member headers, arranged in ascending order.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3648">Chaque décalage est un entier long non signé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3648">Each offset is an unsigned long .</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3649">Le nombre m est égal à la valeur du champ nombre de membres.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3649">The number m is equal to the value of the Number of Members field.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| \* <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3650">4</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3650">4</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3651">Nombre de symboles</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3651">Number of Symbols</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3652">Valeur non signée de type long qui contient le nombre de symboles indexés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3652">An unsigned long that contains the number of symbols indexed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3653">Chaque membre de fichier d’objet définit généralement un ou plusieurs symboles externes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3653">Each object-file member typically defines one or more external symbols.</span></span> <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        |
| \* <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3654">2 \* n</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3654">2 \* n</span></span> <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3655">Index</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3655">Indices</span></span> <br/>           | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3656">Tableau d’index de base 1 (unsigned short) qui mappe les noms de symboles aux décalages de membres d’archive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3656">An array of 1-based indexes (unsigned short ) that map symbol names to archive member offsets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3657">Le nombre n est égal au nombre de champs de symboles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3657">The number n is equal to the Number of Symbols field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3658">Pour chaque symbole qui est nommé dans la table de chaînes, l’élément correspondant dans le tableau d’index fournit un index dans le tableau offsets.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3658">For each symbol that is named in the string table, the corresponding element in the Indices array gives an index into the offsets array.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3659">Le tableau offsets indique à son tour l’emplacement du membre d’archive qui contient le symbole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3659">The offsets array, in turn, gives the location of the archive member that contains the symbol.</span></span> <br/> |
| \* <br/> | \* <br/>     | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3660">Table de chaînes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3660">String Table</span></span> <br/>      | <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3661">Une série de chaînes terminées par le caractère null qui dénomment tous les symboles dans le répertoire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3661">A series of null-terminated strings that name all of the symbols in the directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3662">Chaque chaîne commence immédiatement après l’octet NULL dans la chaîne précédente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3662">Each string begins immediately after the null byte in the previous string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3663">Le nombre de chaînes doit être égal à la valeur du champ nombre de symboles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3663">The number of strings must be equal to the value of the Number of Symbols field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3664">Ce tableau répertorie tous les noms de symboles dans l’ordre lexical croissant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3664">This table lists all the symbol names in ascending lexical order.</span></span> <br/>                                                                             |



 

### <a name="longnames-member"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3665">Membre Longnames</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3665">Longnames Member</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3666">Le nom du membre longnames est « // ».</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3666">The name of the longnames member is "//".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3667">Le membre longnames est une série de chaînes de noms de membres d’archive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3667">The longnames member is a series of strings of archive member names.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3668">Un nom apparaît ici uniquement lorsqu’il n’y a pas assez de place dans le champ nom (16 octets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3668">A name appears here only when there is insufficient room in the Name field (16 bytes).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3669">Le membre longnames est facultatif.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3669">The longnames member is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3670">Il peut être vide avec uniquement un en-tête, ou il peut être complètement absent sans même en-tête.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3670">It can be empty with only a header, or it can be completely absent without even a header.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3671">Les chaînes se terminent par un caractère null.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3671">The strings are null-terminated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3672">Chaque chaîne commence immédiatement après l’octet NULL dans la chaîne précédente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3672">Each string begins immediately after the null byte in the previous string.</span></span>

## <a name="import-library-format"></a><span data-ttu-id="bf294-3673">Format de bibliothèque d’importation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3673">Import Library Format</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3674">Importer l’en-tête</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3674">Import Header</span></span>](#import-header)
- [<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3675">Type d’importation</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3675">Import Type</span></span>](#import-type)

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3676">Les bibliothèques d’importation traditionnelles, autrement dit, les bibliothèques qui décrivent les exportations d’une image pour une utilisation par une autre, suivent généralement la disposition décrite dans la section 7, [format de fichier archive (bibliothèque)](#archive-library-file-format).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3676">Traditional import libraries, that is, libraries that describe the exports from one image for use by another, typically follow the layout described in section 7, [Archive (Library) File Format](#archive-library-file-format).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3677">La principale différence réside dans le fait que les membres de la bibliothèque d’importation contiennent des fichiers Pseudo-objets plutôt que des fichiers réels, dans lesquels chaque membre comprend les contributions de section requises pour créer les tables d’importation décrites dans la section 6,4, la section [. idata](#the-idata-section) l’éditeur de liens génère cette archive lors de la création de l’application d’exportation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3677">The primary difference is that import library members contain pseudo-object files instead of real ones, in which each member includes the section contributions that are required to build the import tables that are described in section 6.4, [The .idata Section](#the-idata-section) The linker generates this archive while building the exporting application.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3678">La section contributions pour une importation peut être déduite à partir d’un petit ensemble d’informations.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3678">The section contributions for an import can be inferred from a small set of information.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3679">L’éditeur de liens peut soit générer les informations complètes et détaillées dans la bibliothèque d’importation pour chaque membre au moment de la création de la bibliothèque, soit écrire uniquement les informations canoniques dans la bibliothèque et laisser l’application qui l’utilise ultérieurement générer les données nécessaires à la volée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3679">The linker can either generate the complete, verbose information into the import library for each member at the time of the library's creation or write only the canonical information to the library and let the application that later uses it generate the necessary data on the fly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3680">Dans une bibliothèque d’importation avec le format long, un seul membre contient les informations suivantes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3680">In an import library with the long format, a single member contains the following information:</span></span>

<dl> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3681">Archiver l’en-tête de membre</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3681">Archive member header</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3682">En-tête de fichier</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3682">File header</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3683">En-têtes de section</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3683">Section headers</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3684">Données qui correspondent à chacun des en-têtes de section</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3684">Data that corresponds to each of the section headers</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3685">Table de symboles COFF</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3685">COFF symbol table</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3686">Chaînes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3686">Strings</span></span>  
  
</dl>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3687">En revanche, une petite bibliothèque d’importation est écrite comme suit :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3687">In contrast, a short import library is written as follows:</span></span>

<dl> <span data-ttu-id="bf294-3688">Archiver l’en-tête de membre</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3688">Archive member header</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3689">Importer l’en-tête</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3689">Import header</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3690">Chaîne de nom d’importation terminée par un caractère null</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3690">Null-terminated import name string</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3691">Chaîne de nom de DLL se terminant par un caractère null</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3691">Null-terminated DLL name string</span></span>  
</dl>

<span data-ttu-id="bf294-3692">Il s’agit d’informations suffisantes pour reconstruire avec précision la totalité du contenu du membre au moment de son utilisation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="bf294-3692">This is sufficient information to accurately reconstruct the entire contents of the member at the time of its use.</span></span>
